                <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 14 (draft based on MS H)</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.1">
                        <label>4.14.1</label> athāta udarāṇāñ cikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.3">
                        <label>4.14.3</label> aṣṭāv udarāṇi pūrvvam uktāṇi
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣv asādhyam baddhagudaṃ pariśrāvi ca | avaśiṣṭāni
                        kṛcchrasādhyāni sarvvāṇy eva pratyākhyāyopakrameta | teṣv ādyaś
                        caturvvarggo bheṣajasādhyaḥ | uttaraḥ śastrasādhyaḥ |
                        kālaprakarṣāt sarvvāṇy eva śastrasādhyāni bhavanti |
                        varjjayitavyāni vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.4">
                        <label>4.14.4</label> udarī tu gurvabhiṣyandirūkṣavidāhyatisnigdhapiśitapariṣekāvagāhān pariharet |
                        śāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmanīvārān nityam aśnīyāt | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.5">
                        <label>4.14.5</label> tatra vātodariṇam vidārigandhādisiddhena sarppiṣā snehayitvā,
                        tilvakavipakvenānulomya citrāphalatailapragāḍhena
                        vidārigandhādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayec ca | sālvaṇenopanāhayed
                        udaraṃ | bhojayec cainam vidārigandhādisiddhena payasā
                        jāṅgalarasena vā | svedayec cābhīkṣṇam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.6">
                        <label>4.14.6</label> pittodariṇaṃ tu madhuragaṇavipakvena
                        sarppiṣā snehayitvā śyāmātrivṛttriphalāvipakvenānulomya
                        śarkkarāmadhughṛtapragāḍhena nyagrodhādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed
                        anuvāsayec ca | pāyasenopanāhayed udaraṃ | bhojayec cainaṃ
                        vidārigandhādisiddhena kṣīreṇa || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.7">
                        <label>4.14.7</label> śleṣmodariṇan tu pippalyādisiddhena sarppiṣā
                        snehayitvā snuhākṣīravipakvena cānulomya
                        trikaṭukamūtratailapragāḍhena muṣkakādikvāthenāsthāpayed
                        anuvāsayec ca | kīkiṇvasarṣapamūlakabījaiś copanāhayed udaraṃ |
                        bhojayec cainan trikaṭukapragāḍhena kulatthayūṣeṇa | pāyasena vā |
                        svedayec cābhīkṣṇaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.8">
                        <label>4.14.8</label> dūṣyodariṇaṃ tu
                        saptalāśaṃkhinīsvarasasiddhena sarppiṣā virecayet | māsam
                        arddhamāsam vā mahāsnuhīvṛkṣakṣīragomūtrasiddhena vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.9">
                        <label>4.14.9</label> gopitānilamūlatvāt sañcitatvāt malasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvodareṣu saṃsanti bahuśas tv anulomanaṃ ||0|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.10">
                        <label>4.14.10</label> ata ūrddhvan sāmānyānyogān vakṣyāmaḥ ||
                        eraṇḍatailam evāharahar mmāsam ekaṃ dvau vā kevalaṃ mūtrayuktaṃ
                        kṣīrayuktaṃ vā sevetodakavarjjī | mahiṣīmūtraṃ kṣīreṇa nirāhāraḥ
                        saptarātraṃ | uṣṭrīkṣīrāhāro vānnapānaparivārivarjjī pakṣaṃ |
                        pippalīr vvā māsaṃ pūrvvoktena vidhānena vāseveta |
                        saindhavājamodanimbasiddham vā nikumbhatailaṃ |
                        ārddrakaṣṭaṅgaṇakṣārapātrārddhasiddham vā | śatapuṣpasiddham vā
                        vātaśūle vacāryaṃ | śṛṅgaverarasavipakvam vā kṣīram āseveta |
                        cavyāśṛṅgaverakalkam vā payasā | saralāmaradārucittrakam eva vā |
                        muruṅgīśālaparṇṇīśyāmāpunarṇṇavājyotiṣkaphalātailam vā kṣīreṇa |
                        svarjjikāhiṃgumiśram pibet | guḍadvitīyo vā harītakīm bhakṣayet |
                        snuhākṣīrapariśrāvitānām vā pippalīnāṃ sahasraṅ kālena |
                        pathyācūrṇṇam vā snuhākṣīraparibhāvitamutkārikām vā paktvā dāpayet
                        | harītakīcūrṇṇaprastham āḍhake ghṛtasyāvāpya
                        khajenābhimathyānuguptan nidhāyārddhamāsaṃ yavapalle vāsayet |
                        tataś coddhṛtya pariśrāvya mahatīharītakīkvāthāmladadhīnyāvāpya
                        vipaced yathāyogam māsam arddhamāsam vā pāyayet | gavye payasi
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīram āvāpya vipacet || vipakvañ cāvatārya śītībhūtaṃ
                        manthānenābhimathya navanītam ādāya bhūyo
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīrakaṣāyeṇaiva saha vipacet | tad yathāyogam māsam
                        arddhamāsam vā pāyayet |
                        cavyacitrakadantyativiṣākuṣṭhaśārivāviḍaṃgatriphalājamodaharidrādāruharidrāśaṃkhinītṛvṛtkaṭukānām
                        arddhakārṣikā bhāgāḥ | rājavṛkṣaphalamajjo 'aṣṭau karṣāḥ |
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīrapale dve | gavāṃ kṣīramūtrayor aṣṭāvaṣṭau palāni |
                        tat sarvvaṃ ghṛtaprasthe samāvāpya vipacet | tathāyogam māsam
                        arddhamāsam vā pāyayet | etāni khalu tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni
                        sarppīṃṣy
                        udaragulmavidradhyaṣṭhīlānāhakuṣṭhonmādāpasmāreṣūpayojyāni |
                        virecanārtham mūtrāsavāriṣṭasurāś cābhīkṣṇam
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīrasambhṛtāḥ seveta | virecanadravyakaṣāyam vā
                        śṛṅgaveradevadārupragāḍhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.11">
                        <label>4.14.11</label> vamanavirecanadravyāṇām palikābhāgāḥ |
                        pippalyādivacādiharidrādiparipaṭhitānāñ ca dravyāṇāṃ
                        ślakṣṇapiṣṭānāṃ yathoktānāñ ca lavaṇānān tat sarvvam mūtragaṇe
                        prakṣipya mahāvṛkṣakṣīraprasthañ ca mṛdvagnināvaghaṭṭayan vipacet
                        | avidagdhakalkan tatsādhusiddham avatārya śītībhūtam
                        aṅguṣṭhamātrāṅ guṭikām varttayet | tāsām ekāṃ dve tisro vā yathāyogam māsām̐s trīṃś caturo vā
                        seveta | eṣā khalu mūtravarttikriyāviśeṣeṇa mahāvyādhiṣūpayujyate
                        | koṣṭhajām̐ś ca krimīn upahanti
                        kāsaśvāsapratiśyāyārocakāvipākodāvarttām̐ś ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.12">
                        <label>4.14.12</label>
                        madanaphalamajjājīmūtakekṣvākutrikaṭukasarṣapalavaṇāni
                        mūtrakṣārayor anyatareṇa piṣṭvāṅguṣṭhamātrāvarttī kṛtvodariṇaḥ |
                        ānāhe tu tailalavaṇagudābhyaktasyaikāṃ dve ca pāyau nidadhyāt |
                        eṣānāhavarttikriyā vātamūtrapurīṣodāvarttādhmānānāheṣu vidheyā |
                        dūṣyodariṇan tu vyoṣāśvamārakaguñjākākādanīmūlakalkam pāyayet |
                        ikṣukāṇḍāni vā kṛṣṇasarpeṇa daṃśayitvā bhakṣayet | vallīphalāni vā
                        kandajam vā mūlajam vā viṣam āseveta | tenāgadībhavaty anyataram
                        vā bhāvam āpadyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.13">
                        <label>4.14.13</label> plīhodariṇas tūpasnigdhasvinnasya dadhnā
                        bhuktavato vāmabāhukurpparasandhāv abhyantarasirām vidhyet |
                        vimarddayec ca pāṇinā plīhānaṃ | rudhiraprasyandanārthan tataḥ
                        śuddhadehaṃ samudraśuktikṣāram payasā pāyayeta | hiṅgusauvarccikām
                        vā kṣīreṇa | śrutena vā palāśakṣāreṇa |
                        yavakṣārapārijātakekṣurakāpāmārggakṣāram vā tailasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ |
                        saubhāñjanakayūṣaṃ vā pippalīsaindhavacitrakayuktam
                        amlapūtikarañjakṣāram vā | viḍaṅgalavaṇapippalīprāgāḍhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.14">
                        <label>4.14.14</label> pippalīpippalīmūlaṃ
                        śṛṅgaveracitrakayavakṣārasaindhavānām palikā bhāgāḥ |
                        ghṛtaprasthaṃ tattulyaṃ kṣīran tadekadhyam vipācayed etat khalu
                        ṣaṭpalakaṃ
                        plīhāgnisādagulmodāvarttaśvayathupāṇḍurogaśvāsakāsapratiśyāyor
                        ddhvavātaviṣamajvarān upahanti ||
                        pipplalīmaricaśṛṅgaverahiṅgusaindhavasauvarccalaviḍadāḍimayavānikāpuṣkaramūlājājīdhānyāmlavetasakṣāradvayavacācittrakailājagandhātulasītyetaiḥ
                        samair ghṛtaprasthan dadhi caturgguṇaṃ bījapūrakarasayuktam
                        pācayed etad dādhikaṃ sarppir ddīpanīyam
                        udaragulmakāsaśvāsajvaravidradyaṣṭhīlānāhasarvvavātarukchamanaṃ
                        śūlaghnañ ceti ||
                        śṛṅgaveramātuluṅgarasadāḍimadadhiśuṣkamūlakolāmlakaṣāyaprastheṣu
                        ghṛtaprasthañ cāvāpya | pañca
                        kolaviḍaṅgayavānīśuṣkamūlapāṭhagarbbhan tan siddham pāyayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.15">
                        <label>4.14.15</label> yakṛddālye 'py eṣa eva kriyāvibhāgaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣatas tu dakṣiṇabāhau sirām vidhyet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.16">
                        <label>4.14.16</label> maṇibandhe samunnāmya vāmam aṅguṣṭham
                        īritaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dahet sirāṃ śareṇāśu plīho vaidyaḥ praśāntaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.17">
                        <label>4.14.17</label> baddhagude parisrāvini ca
                        snigdhasvinnasyādho nābher vvāmataś caturaṅgulam apahāya
                        romarājyād udaraṃ pāṭayitvā caturaṅgulapramāṇamantrāṇi niṣkṛṣya
                        nirīkṣya baddhagudasyāntrapratirodhakaramasmānaṃ bālam vāpohya
                        malajātan tato madhu sarppiṣābhyajyāntrāṇi yathāsthānaṃ
                        sthāpayitvā bāhyaṃ vraṇam udarasya sīvyet | parisrāviṇo py evam
                        antraṃ samānayitvā cchidraṃ kālapipīlikābhir ddaṅśayet | daṣṭe ca
                        tāsāṃ kāyān upaharec chinnaśirāṃsi tataḥ pūrvvavat sīvyet |
                        vāsayec cainan tailadroṇyām alpam vā payovṛttir iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.18">
                        <label>4.14.18</label> udakodariṇas tu
                        tailābhyaktasyoṣṇodakaparisvinnasyāptaiḥ suparigṛhītasyākakṣāt
                        paṭūveṣṭitasyārdho nābheś caturaṅgulam apahāya
                        romarāmāṇyardvyaṅgulam vrīhimukhenāṅguṣṭhodaramātram vidārya
                        trapvādīnām anyatamasya nāḍīm ubhayato dvāraṃ saṃyojya doṣodakam
                        avasiñcen na caikasmin divase sarvvadoṣodakam apaharet ||
                        sahasāpahyate doṣe tṛṣṇājvarāṅgamarddātīsāraśvāsakāsapādadāhā
                        utpadyeran | āpūryate vā dṛḍhataram asañjātaprāṇasya tasmāt
                        tṛtīyañ caturtham pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭham aṣṭamam vā dvādaśam vā divasam
                        antaraṃ doṣodakam alpam alpam avasiñcet | nisrute nisrute doṣe
                        gāḍhataram āvikakauṣeyacarmmaṇām anyatamena pariveṣṭayed udaran
                        tathā nādhmāpayati vāyuḥ ṣaṇmāsām̐ś ca bhojayet payasā rasena vā |
                        tatas trīn māsānavodakena phalāmlena vāvaśiṣṭam māsatrayam annaṃ
                        laghu hitaṃ seveta evaṃ samvatsareṇāgadībhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.19">
                        <label>4.14.19</label> bhavati cātra||
                        <caesura/>
                         āsthāpane caiva virecane ca pāne tathāhāravidhikriyāsu |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvodarāṇāṃ kuśalena yojyaṃ kṣīraṃ raso jāṅgalajo tha vā syād
                        iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.1"><label>4.15.1</label> athāto
                        mūḍhagarbhbhacikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.3"><label>4.15.3</label> nātaḥ kaṣṭataramasti yathā
                        mūḍhagarbhbhoddharaṇamatra hi yoniyakṛtplīhāntragarbhbhāśayānām
                        madhye kartavyaṃ | sparśeno
                        tkarṣāyakarṣaṇāpakarttanabhedanavyāvarttanapīḍanārjjūkaraṇāni
                        caikahastena garbhbhamahiṃsatā garbhbhiṇīñ cāhiṃsatā tasmād
                        adhikṛtya tam āpṛcchya parañ ca yan namāsthāyopakrameta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.4"><label>4.15.4</label> tatra samāsenāṣṭavidha
                        mūḍhagarbhbhagatiruddiṣṭā svabhāvagatā vapi tu trayaḥ saṅgā
                        bhavanti śiraso vaipulyādaṃśayor jjaghanasya vā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.5"><label>4.15.5</label> jīvati garbhbhe sūtyaḥ
                        prayateran |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirharaṇe cyāvanāṃś ca mantrānanuśrāvayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.6"><label>4.15.6</label> ihāmṛtaś ca somaś ca
                        citrabhānuś ca bhāvini |
                        <caesura/>
                         uccaiḥśravāś ca turago mandire nivasantu te || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.7"><label>4.15.7</label> idamamṛtamapāṃ samuddhṛtāṃ
                        vai tava laghu garbhbhamimam pramuñcahe stri |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad analapavanārkkavāsavās te saha lavaṇāmbudharair ddiśantu
                        śāntiṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.8"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.9"><label>4.15.9</label> oṣadhāni ca vidadhyād
                        yathoktāni ca | mṛte cottānāyā bhugnasakthinyā
                        vastracumbhalakonnāmitakaṭyā
                        dhanvakamṛttikāśālmalīmṛtsnaghṛtābhyām mrakṣayitvā hastaṃ yonyām
                        praveśya garbhbham apaharet tatra śakthibhyām āgatam anulomam
                        evāñchet | ekasakthi pratipannasyetaraṃ sakthi prasārya
                        sphigdeśāgataṃ sphigdeśaṃ prapīḍyorddhvam utkṣipya sakthinī
                        prasāryasyāpaharet | tiryag āgatasya parighasyeva tiryak cīnasya
                        paścād arddhamūrddham utkṣipya pūrvvārddham apatyapathaṃ
                        pratyārjjavamānayitvāpaharet | dvāvanty āvasādhyau mūḍhagarbhbhau
                        bhavataḥ | evam aśakye śastram avatārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.10"><label>4.15.10</label> sacetanan tu śastreṇa na
                        kathañcana dārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ātmānañ jananīñ caiva hanyād āśu sacetanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.11"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.12"><label>4.15.12</label> tataḥ striyam āśvāsya
                        maṇḍalāgreṇāṅguliśastreṇa vā śiro vidārya śiraḥkapālāny āhṛtya
                        śaṃkunā saṃgṛhyor asi kakṣe cāpaharet | abhinnaśiram vākṣikūṭo
                        gaṇḍe vā asaṃsaktasyāṃśadeśe bāhūṃ cchhitvā dṛtim ivātatam
                        vātapūrṇṇodaram vidārya nirasyātrāṇi śithilībhūtāṃ |
                        jaghanaśaktasya vā jaghanakapālānīti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.13"><label>4.15.13</label> yasminn aṅge hi yo

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.39"><label>4.15.39</label> etad dhirājñāṅ

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.40"><label>4.15.40</label> balākaṣāyapītebhyas
                        tilebhyo vā py anekaśaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tailam utpādya tat tailaṃ śatapākakṛtaṃ śubhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.41"><label>4.15.41</label> śaste 'hni
                        nibhṛtaveśmany upayuñjyād yathābalaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         jīrṇṇesmin payasā siddhaṃ ṣaṣṭikānnam avāpnuyāt | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.42"><label>4.15.42</label> anena vidhinā droṇam
                        upayuñjyānnamīritaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bhuñjīta dviguṇaṃ kālaṃ balavarṇṇānvitas tataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.43"><label>4.15.43</label> sarvvapāpair
                        vvinirmmuktaḥ śatāyuḥ puruṣo bhavet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śataṃ śataṃ cotkarṣād droṇe droṇe prakīrttyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.44"><label>4.15.44</label>
                        balākalpenātibalāguḍūcyādity avalliṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         śairīyake vīratare śatāvaryān trikaṇṭake || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.45"><label>4.15.45</label> tailāni kuryāt
                        madhukaprasāraṇyoś ca buddhimān | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.46"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.47"><label>4.15.47</label> sarvveṣām eva caiteṣām
                        upayogañ cikitsakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         balātailavadācaṣṭe guṇāṃś caivā viśeṣata iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.1">
                        <label>4.17.1</label>athāto visarppanāḍīstanarogāṇāñ cikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.3">
                        <label>4.17.3</label>sādhyā visarppās traya ādito ye tat
                        sannipātakṣatajāvasādhyau |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyeṣu pathyair hi gaṇair vvidadhyād ghṛtāvasekoś ca tathā
                        pradehān ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.4">
                        <label>4.17.4</label>kuṣṭhaṃ
                        śatāhvāsuradārumustāvārāhikustuṃvurukṛṣṇagandhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāterkkavaṃśārttagaṇās tu yojyā sekeṣu lepeṣu tathā ghṛteṣu
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.5">
                        <label>4.17.5</label>yat pañcamūlaṃ khalu kaṇṭakākhyam alpam mahac
                        cāpy athavallijāñ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         taccopayojyam bhiṣajā pradehaiḥ seke ghṛte cāpi tathaiva taile
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.6">
                        <label>4.17.6</label>kaseruśṛṅgāṭakapadmagundrāḥ saśaivalāḥ
                        sotpalakarddamām̐ś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vastrāntarā pittakṛte visarppalepāvidheyāḥ saghṛtāḥ suśītāḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.7">
                        <label>4.17.7</label>hrīveralāmajjakacandanāni
                        śrotojamuktāmaṇigairikaiś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrābhipiṣṭāḥ saghṛtāḥ suśītā lepāḥ prayojyās tanavaḥ sukhāya
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.8">
                        <label>4.17.8</label>mañjīṣṭhayaṣṭīmadhukam payasyāprapauṇḍarīkaṃ
                        saha padmakena |
                        <caesura/>
                         saugandhikāñ ceti sukhapralepaḥ paitte visarppe bhiṣajā prayojyāḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.9">
                        <label>4.17.9</label>nyagrodhavarggam pariṣecanañ ca ghṛtañ ca
                        kuryāt svarasena tasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītaiḥ payo bhiś ca madhūdakaiś ca saśarkkarair ikṣurasaiś ca
                        sekāṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.10">
                        <label>4.17.10</label>ghṛtañ ca
                        gaurīmadhukāravindalodhrāmvurājādanajīvakeṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathārṣabhe padmakaśārivāyāṃ kākoli2medākumudotpaleṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.11">
                        <label>4.17.11</label>sacandanāyām madhuśarkkarāyān
                        drākṣāsthirāpṛṣṇisamaṅgayā ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkīkṛtāsūdakamatragandhā nyagrodhavarggasya ca śārivādeḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.12">
                        <label>4.17.12</label>gaṇasya vilvādikapañcamūlyoś caturgguṇaṃ
                        kṣīramathāpi tadvat |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasthaṃ vipakvaṃ pariṣecanena paittāni hanyāt tu visapppanāḍī
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.13">
                        <label>4.17.13</label>visphoṭaduṣṭavraṇaśīrṣarogān pākan
                        tathāsyāsya tathaiva pānāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         grahārddite śoṣiṇi cāpi vāle | ghṛtaṃ tu gaurādikam etad iṣṭaṃ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.14">
                        <label>4.17.14</label>athāśvagandhā saralātha kālā
                        saikeṣikāvāpyathavājaśṛṅgī |
                        <caesura/>
                         gomūtrapiṣṭo vihimapradeho hanyādvisarppaṅkaphajaṃ suśīghraṃ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.15"
                        >kālānusāryāgurucocaguñjārasnāvacāśītaśivendraparṇṇyaḥ |

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.16">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.17">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.36">
                        <label>4.17.36</label>varāhaviṭsūkṣmamasīpradeyā nāḍīṣu tailena
                        vimiśrayitvā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.38">
                        <label>4.17.38</label>tathā ca gomāṃsamasīṃ hitāya koṣṭhāśritā
                        svādarato diśanti |.
                        <caesura/>
                         varttīkṛtam mākṣikasaṃprayuktan nāḍīghnamuktaṃ lavaṇottamam vā
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.39">
                        <label>4.17.39</label>duṣṭavraṇe yad vihitaṃ ca tailan tat
                        sevyamānaṅ gatim āśu hanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.37">
                        <label>4.17.37</label>dhattūrakam madanakodravajañ ca vījaṃ
                        kośātakī śukanasā mṛgabhojinī ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāṅkollavījakusumais tu kṛtañ ca cūrṇṇaṃ lākṣodakāhṛtamalāsu
                        gatīṣu deyaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.40">
                        <label>4.17.40</label>eṣv eva sādhuṣu kṛteṣu vimiśrayitvā tailaṃ
                        kṛtaṅ gatim apohati saptarātrāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṇḍīkṛtasya tu varāhavibhāvitasya mūleṣu kandaśakaleṣu ca
                        sauvaheṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.41">
                        <label>4.17.41</label>tailaṅ kṛtaṅ gatim apohati śīghram eva
                        kandeṣu cāmaravarāyudhasāhvayeṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhallātakārkkamaricair llavaṇottamena siddhaṃ
                        viḍaṃgarajanīdvayacitrakair yat ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.42">
                        <label>4.17.42</label>syāmārkkavasya ca rasena nihanti tailaṃ
                        nāḍīṃ kaphānilakṛtānapacīn vraṇām̐ś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         stanye gate vikṛtim āśu bhiṣak tu dhātrīṃ pītvā ghṛtaṃ
                        pariṇatehani vāmayīta ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.43">
                        <label>4.17.43</label>nimvodakena madhumāgadhikāyutena vāntāpare
                        'hani ca mudgarasāsanā syāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         evan tryahañ caturahaṃ ṣaḍaham vamed vā sarppiḥ pived triphalayā
                        saha saṃyutam vā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.44">
                        <label>4.17.44</label>bhārggīm vacām ativiṣāṃ suradārupāṭhām
                        mustādikam madhurasāṅ kaṭurohiṇīñ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhātrī pivet tu payasaḥ pariśodhanārtha mustāvacādi tu varam
                        madhunātha vāpi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.45">
                        <label>4.17.45</label>stanarogam utthitam avekṣya bhiṣag vidadhyād
                        yad vidradhāvabhihitam vahudhābhidhānam ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.46"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.47">
                        <label>4.17.47</label>āme vidahyati tathaiva gate ca pākan tasyā
                        stanau satatam eva ca nirdduhīteti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">.. cikitsā <unclear extent="2" unit="syllables"/>.. o
                        ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="18" type="adhyāya" corresp="4.18 in NAK 5-333">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 18 (draft based on MS H)</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.1">
                        <label>4.18.1</label> athāto granthyapacyarbbudagalagaṇḍānāñ
                        cikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.3">
                        <label>4.18.3</label> granthiṣv athāmeṣu bhiṣag vidadhyāc
                        chophakriyā vistaraśo vidhijñaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.3a">
                        <label>4.18.3a</label> rakṣed balañ cāpi narasya nityaṃ tad
                        rakṣitam vyādhibalan nihanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.4">
                        <label>4.18.4</label> tailaṃ pibet sarppiratha dvayaṃ vā datvā
                        vasām vā trivṛtam vidadhyāt| apīhavātedaśamūlasiddhaṃ
                        vaidyaścatuḥsnehamathāpi dadyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.5">
                        <label>4.18.5</label> hiṃsrāsa rohiṇyamṛtātha bharggī
                        śyonākabilvāgurukṛṣṇagandhā | gojī ca piṣṭā saha tālapattryā
                        granthau vidheyā nilaje pralepaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.6">
                        <label>4.18.6</label> svedopanāhā vividhāś ca yojyāḥ kuryāt
                        prasiddhānaparāṃś ca lepān| vidārya pakvaṃ samupohya pūyam
                        prakṣālya bilvārkkagaṇaditoyaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.7">
                        <label>4.18.7</label> tilaiḥ sapañcāṅgulapattramiśraiḥ saṃśodhayet
                        saindhavasaṃprayuktaiḥ| śuddham vraṇañ cāpy uparopayīta tailena
                        rāsnāsaralāyutena|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.8">
                        <label>4.18.8</label> viḍaṅgayaṣṭīmadhukāmṛtābhiḥ siddhena taṃ
                        kṣīravimiśritena| jalāyukāḥ pittakṛte hitās tu kṣīrodakābhyām
                        pariṣecanañ ca|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.9">
                        <label>4.18.9</label> kākolivarggasya tu śītalāni pibet kaṣāyāṇi
                        saśarkka-rāṇi| drākṣārasenekṣurasena vāpi cūrṇṇaṃ pibed vāpi
                        harītakīnāṃ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.10">
                        <label>4.18.10</label> madhūkajambvarjjunavetasānāṃ tvagbhiḥ
                        pradehānavacārayecca| saśarkkarair vvā
                        tṛṇaśūlyakandairddihyādabhīkṣṇaṃ mucilindajair vvā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.11">
                        <label>4.18.11</label> vidārya vā pakvamapohya pūyaṃ dhāvet
                        kaṣāyeṇa vanaspatīnāṃ| tilaiḥ sayaṣṭīmadhukairvviśodhya sarppiḥ
                        prayojyam madhurairvvipakvaṃ|| </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.12">
                        <label>4.18.12</label> hṛteṣu doṣeṣu yathānupūrvvā granthau bhiṣak
                        chleṣmasamutthiteṣu | svinnasya vimlāpanam eva kuryād
                        aṃguṣṭhaveṇudṛśadīsutais tu|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.13">
                        <label>4.18.13</label>
                        vikaṃkatāragvadhakākaṇantīkākādanītāpasavṛkṣamūlaiḥ| ālepayed
                        enama lāvubhārggīkarañjakālāmadanaiś ca vidvān|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.14">
                        <label>4.18.14</label> amarmmaje cānupa śīmymānasapakvam
                        evāpahared vidārya| dahet sthite cāsṛji siddhakarmmā sadyaḥ
                        kṣatoktañ ca vidhim vidadhyāt|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.15">
                        <label>4.18.15</label> yā māṃsakandyaḥ kaṭhinā bṛhatyastāsvapya
                        yaṃ karmma vidhiḥ prayojyaḥ| śastreṇa cāpāṭya vipakvamāśu
                        prakṣālayet pathyatamaiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.16">
                        <label>4.18.16</label> saṃśodhanais tañ ca viśodhayīta
                        kṣārottamaiḥ kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhaiḥ| śuddhe ca tailaṃ
                        tvavacāraṇīyam viḍaṅgapāṭhārajanīvipakvaṃ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.17">
                        <label>4.18.17</label> medaḥsamutthe tilakalkadigdhaṃ
                        tvacopariṣṭād dviguṇam paṭāntaṃ| hutāśataptena muhuḥ
                            pramṛjyā<unclear extent="1" unit="char"/>lena dhīmānadahan
                        hitāya|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.18">
                        <label>4.18.18</label> pralipya dārvvīmatha lākṣayā vā prataptayā
                        svedanam asya kāryaṃ| nipātya vā śastramapohya medo dahet supakvan
                        tv athavā vidārya|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.19">
                        <label>4.18.19</label> prakṣālya mūtraiś ca tilaiḥ supiṣṭaiḥ
                        suvarccikādyair haritālamisraiḥ| sasaindhavaiḥ
                        kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhaiḥ kṣārottarair enam abhipraśodhya|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.20">
                        <label>4.18.20</label> tailaṃ vidadyād
                        dvikaraṃjaguñjāvaṅgāvalekheṅgudimūtra-siddhaiḥ| jīmūtakī
                        kośavatīphaleṣu dantī dravantī trivṛtāsu caiva|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.21">
                        <label>4.18.21</label> sarppiḥ kṛtaṃ hanty apacīṃ pravṛddhāṃ
                        dvidhā pravṛttan tad udāravīryaṃ| nirgguṇḍijātībarihiṣṭhayuktaṃ
                        jīmūtakaṃ mākṣikasaindhavāḍhyaṃ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.22">
                        <label>4.18.22</label> abhiprataptaṃ vamanaṃ praśastaṃ
                        duṣṭāpacīṣūttamamādiśanti| nirgguṇḍi bimbīkaravīrasiddhaṃ tailaṃ
                        hitaṃ śīrṣavirecanaṃ ca|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.23">
                        <label>4.18.23</label> śākhoṭakalka svarasena siddhaṃ tailaṃ hitaṃ
                        nasyaniśevanena| madhūkasāraś ca hito vapīḍe phalāni śigroḥ
                        kharamañjarervvā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.24">
                        <label>4.18.24</label> granthīnamarmmaprabhavānapakvānuddhṛtya
                        cāgniṃ vidadhīta vaidyaḥ| kṣāreṇa cainaṃ pratisārayīt
                        muhurmmhurllikhyama thoyathāvat|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.25">
                        <label>4.18.25</label> pārṣṇim prati dvā daśa cāṅgulāni
                        mātvendrabastim parivarjjya dhīmān| vidārya matsyāṇḍanibhāni
                        vaidyo jālāni niḥkramyavidhimviddhyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.26"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.27">
                        <label>4.18.27</label> maṇibandhopariṣṭādvā kuryād rekhātrayam bhiṣak| aṅgulāntaritaṃ
                        samyag apacīnāṃ nivṛttaye|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.28">
                        <label>4.18.28</label> cūrṇṇasya kāle
                        parcalākakākagodhāhikūrmmaprabhavās tumaṣyaḥ | dadyāc ca tailena
                        saheṅgudīnāṃ tailāni vakṣyāmi ca ślīpadeṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.29">
                        <label>4.18.29</label> vairecanan dhūmam upādadīta bhavec ca
                        nityaṃ yavamudgabhojī| karkkāruker
                        vvārukanālikerapiyālapañcāṅgulabījapūrṇṇaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.30">
                        <label>4.18.30</label> vātārbbudaṃ kṣīraghṛtāmbusiddhair uṣṇaiḥ
                        satailair upanāhayettu| kuryāc ca mukhyānuupanāhanārtham bhṛteṣu
                        māṃseṣu ca veśavārāṃ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.31">
                        <label>4.18.31</label> svedam vidadhyāt kuśalantu nāḍyā śṛṅgena
                        raktam bahuśo harecca| vātaghnaniryūhapayomlabhāgaiḥ siddhaṃ
                        śatākhya trivṛtam pibedvā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.32">
                        <label>4.18.32</label> svedo-panāhā mṛduvas tu pathyāḥ pittārbbude
                        kāyavirecanañ ca| vighṛṣya codumbari kākagojīpatrairbhbhṛśaṃ
                        kṣaudrayutaiḥ pralimpet|| </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.33">
                        <label>4.18.33</label> sūkṣṇīkṛtaiḥ
                        sarjjarasapriyaṃgū-pattaṅgalodhrāñjanayaṣṭikāhvaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāvya cāragvadhagojisomāḥ śyāmā va yojyāḥ kuśalena lepaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.34">
                        <label>4.18.34</label> śyāmāgirihvārajanīraseṣu drākṣārase
                        saptalikārase ca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtaṃ pacet klītakajecasiddhaṃ pittārbudī tajjaṭhare ca jantuḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.35">
                        <label>4.18.35</label> śuddhaś ca jantoḥ kaphaje rbude tu rakte
                        'vasikte ca tato 'rbudan tat |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkair ddihed ūrddhvamadhaś ca yani dravyāṇi doṣānapaciṃ nudanti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.36">
                        <label>4.18.36</label> kapotapārāvataviḍvimiśraiḥ sakāṃśanīlī
                        śukalāṅgalākhyaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūlais tu kākādanimūlamisraiḥ kṣārapradigdhair athavā pradihyāt
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.37">
                        <label>4.18.37</label> niṣpāvapiṇyākakulatthakalkair
                        mmāṃsapragāḍhair ddadhimardditais tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         lepaṃ vidadhyāt krimayo yathātra mūrcchanti muñcanty atha makṣikā
                        vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.38">
                        <label>4.18.38</label> alpāvaśiṣṭaṃ krimibhakṣitan tallikhettato
                        'gnim vidadhīta paścāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         yadalpamūlaṃ trapuśīsatāsrais tadveṣṭya paṭṭair athavāyasair vvā
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.39">
                        <label>4.18.39</label> kṣārāgniśastrāṇyavacārayīta muhur mmuhuḥ
                        prāṇamahiṃsamānaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āsphotajātīkaravīrapatraiḥ kaṣāyam iṣṭaṃ vraṇaśodhanārthaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.40">
                        <label>4.18.40</label> śuddhe ca tailaṃ vidadhīta
                        bhārggīviḍaṅgapāṭhātriphalāsusiddhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yadṛcchayā- copagatāni pākaṃ krameṇa caivaopacaredvidhijñaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.41">
                        <label>4.18.41</label> medo 'rbbudaṃ svedya vidārya saudhya
                        sīvyādyathoktaṃ gataraktamāśu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato haridrāgṛhadhūmalodhrapattaṅgacūrṇṇaiḥ samanaḥ śilālaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.42">
                        <label>4.18.42</label> vraṇam pratigrāha madhupragāḍhaiḥ
                        karañjatailaṃ vidadhīta śuddhe |
                        <caesura/>
                         saśeṣadoṣāṇi hi yo 'rbbudāni karoti tānyāśu punar bhbhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.43">
                        <label>4.18.43</label> tasmād aśeṣāṇi samuddharet tu hanyuḥ
                        saśeṣāṇi yathā viṣāgnī |
                        <caesura/>
                         svinne 'nilothaṃ galagaṇḍamadau nāḍyāni laghnauṣadhapatrabhaṅgaiḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.44">
                        <label>4.18.44</label> amleṣu pattraiṣu payaḥ sucāpi svedaṃ
                        vidaddhyāt piśiteṣu cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāvayet svinnam atandritas tu rūḍhaṃ vraṇaṃ cāpy upanāhayīta
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.45">
                        <label>4.18.45</label> śaṇātasīmūlakeśigrusidgraiḥ
                        piyālamajjāsahitais tilais tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         kālāmṛtāśigrupunarnnavārkkagajādināmākaraghāṭakuṣṭhaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.46">
                        <label>4.18.46</label> ekai-ṣikāvṛkṣakatilvakaiś ca surāmlapiṣṭaiḥ
                        pradihedabhīkṣṇaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.47">
                        <label>4.18.47</label> tailam
                        pibeccāmṛtavallinimbahansāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ sahadeva-dāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.48">
                        <label>4.18.48</label> svedopanāhaiḥ kaphasambhavan tu saṃsvedaya
                        visrāvaṇam eva kuryāt ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tato 'jagandhātiviṣāviśalyāviṣāṇikālāvuśukā-ñjānāśā kecit
                        pāṭhahvayābhiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.49">
                        <label>4.18.49</label> palāśabhasmodakapeśitābhir ddihyāt
                        suguñjābhir aśītalābhiḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         daśārddhaśaṅkhair llavaṇaiś ca yuktaṃ tailaṃ
                        pibetmāgadhikādisiddhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.50">
                        <label>4.18.50</label> praccharddanaṃ śīrṣavirecanañ ca dhūpaś tu
                        vair ecaniko hitas tu ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pākakramo vā pyanayo vidheyo vaidyena pākaṃgatayo kathañcit | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.51">
                        <label>4.18.51</label> kaṭutrikakṣaudrayutāś ca śastā bhakṣyā
                        yavānnāni rasāś ca maudgāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saśṛṃgaverāḥ sapaṭolanimbā hitāya deyā galagaṇḍaroge | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.52">
                        <label>4.18.52</label> medaḥsamutthe tu yathopadiṣṭāṃ vidhyet
                        sirāṃ snigdhatanornnarasya ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmāsudhālohapurīṣadantīrasāñjanaiś cāpi hitaḥ pralepaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.53">
                        <label>4.18.53</label> mūtreṇa cāloḍya hitāya kalkaṃ prātaḥ pibet
                        sāramahīruhāṇāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śastreṇa vā 'pāṭya vidārite ca medaḥ samuddhṛtya hitāya sīvyet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.54">
                        <label>4.18.54</label> majjāvasākṣadrayutair ddahedvā dagdhe ca
                        sarppirmmadhu cāvacāryaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīsatutthe ca tato 'tra deye cūrṇṇīkṛte rocanayā ca yukte | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.55">
                        <label>4.18.55</label> tailena cābhyajya hitāya dadyāt sārodbhavaṃ
                        gomayajañ ca bhasma |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitañ ca nityan triphalākaṣāyaṃ gā ḍhaś ca bandho yavabhojanañ
                        ceti ||</l>

                <div n="19" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 19]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.1"> athāto vṛddhyupadaṃśaślīpadānāṃ cikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.3"> antravṛddhim ṛte ye 'nye vṛddhayas teṣu
                        varjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vegāghātaṃ pṛṣṭhayānaṃ vyāyāmaṃ maithunaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.4"> anaśanaṃ cātyaśanam adhyaśanam atho guruḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrādito vātavṛddhau trivṛtāsnigdham āturam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.5"> sninnañ caiva yathānyāyam pāyayīta virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kośāmratilvakair aṇḍaphalatailāni vā naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.6"> sakṣīram vā pibet māsaṃ tailam eraṇḍasambhavaṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kāle 'nilaghnānāṃ kvāthaiḥ kalkaiś ca buddhimān || </l>

                        jalaukābhir upācaret |

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.10"><label>4.21.10</label> avamanthe gate pākaṃ
                        bhinne tailaṃ vidhīyate |

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.11"><label>4.21.11</label> kriyām puṣkarikāyāṃ tu

                    <head>[Adhyāya 23]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.1"><label>4.23.1</label>athātaḥ śophacikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.3"><label>4.23.3</label>tatra
                        ṣaḍvidhovayavasamutthaḥ śophobhihito lakṣaṇataḥ pratikārataś ca |
                        sarvasaraś ca pañcavidhaḥ | tad yathā |
                        vātapittakaphasaṃnipātaviṣannimittaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.4"
                        ><label>4.23.4</label>tatrāpatarpitasyābhyarthamadhvagamanādatimātramabhyaharato
                        vā piṣṭānnaharitaśākalavaṇāni | kṣīṇasya vātimātramamlam upasevato
                        mṛtpaktaloṣṭakaṭaśarkarām upaudakamāṃsasevito vā viruddhāhārasya
                        hastyaśvakṣobhanādāyāsitā doṣā dhātūṃ pradūṣayitvā
                        śophamāpādayantyakhile śarīre |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.5"><label>4.23.5</label>tatra
                        vātapittakaphasannipātaśvayathūnām avayavasamutthe śophalakṣaṇāni
                        vyākhyātāni | viṣanimittas tu garopayogāddu ṣṭatoyasevanāt
                        prakuthitodakāvasekāt saviṣasatvasañcūrṇṇanād vā |
                        saviṣamūtrapurīśaśukraspṛṣṭānāṃ vā tṛṇakāṣṭhādīnāṃ saṃsparśāt ||
                        sa tu mṛduḥ kṣiprotthām ca lāvalamvī dāhapākaprāyaś ca bhavati
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.6"><label>4.23.6</label>doṣāḥ śvayathumūrdhvaṃ hi
                        kurvantyāmāśayāśritāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvāśayasthā madhye tu varcasthānagatāstvadhaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.7"><label>4.23.7</label>kṛtsnaṃ dehamanuprāptāḥ |
                        kuryuḥ sarvasaran tathā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yo madhyadeśe śvayathuḥ sa kaṣṭaḥ sarvagaś ca yaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.8"><label>4.23.8</label>ardhāṅgeriṣṭabhūtaṃ syād
                        yaścordhvaṃ parisarpati |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaḥ pipāsācchardiś ca daurvalyaṃ jvara eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.9"><label>4.23.9</label>yasya cānnerucir nāsti
                        śvayathuṃ taṃ vivarjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi bheṣajaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.10"><label>4.23.10</label>tatra śophinaḥ sarva eva
                        parihareyuḥ |amlalavaṇamadyaguḍadadhivasātailapiṣṭagurūṇi viśeṣeṇa
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.11"><label>4.23.11</label>tatra vātaśvayathau
                        trivṛttairaṇḍatailaṃ vā māsam arddhamāsam vā pāyayet | nyagrodhādi
                        siddhaṃ sarpiḥ | pittaśvayathau | āragvadhādisiddhaṃ tailaṃ
                        śleṣmaśvayathau | sannipāśvayathau snuhākṣīrapātratulyaṃ daśabhir
                        amlapātraiḥ | pratisaṃsṛjya dantī dravantī pra tivāyaṃ sarpiḥ
                        pācayitvā pāyayet | viṣanimittamākalpeṣu pratīkāraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.12"><label>4.23.12</label>ata ūrdhvaṃ samānyān yogā
                        vakṣyāmaḥ |tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni yānyuktāni udareṣu tatonyatamam
                        upayujyamānaṃ śvayathūnapahanti | mūrttavarttikriyām vā seveta |
                        navāyasaṃ vāharaharmadhunā |
                        viḍaṅgātiviṣākuṭajaphalabhadradārunāgaramaricānāṃ vā
                        dharaṇamuṣṇāmvunā | trikaṭukakṣārayaścūrṇāni triphalākvāthena |
                        mūtram vā tulyakṣīraṃ | harītakīm vā tulyaguḍām upayuñjīta |
                        devadāruśuṇṭhīṃ vā | guggulum vā mūtreṇa | varṣābhūkaṣāyānupānam
                        vā tulyaguḍaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ | vyoṣaṃ varṣābhūkaṣāyasiddhena vā |
                        sarpiṣāmudgolumvāṃ bhakṣayet |
                        pippalīmūlacitrakacavyāmayūrakavarṣābhūsiddhaṃ vā kṣīraṃ pivet |
                        sahauṣadhamuraṅgīmūlasiddham vā | trikacukair aṇḍaśyāmāmūlasiddham
                        vā | varṣābhūśṛṃgaveradevadārusiddham vā |
                        tathālāvuvibhītakaphalakalkam vā |
                        pippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverānusiddhena ca mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpaṃ snehaṃ
                        bhojayet | yavagodhūmānnaṃ |
                        vṛkṣakārkanaktamālanimvavarṣābhūkvāthaś ca pariṣekaḥ |
                        sarṣapasauvarcalasaindhavaśārṅge ṣṭābhiś ca pradehaḥ kāryaḥ |
                        yathādoṣañ ca tīkṣṇānivamanavirecanāsthāpanānuvāsanāni satatam
                        upaseveta | svedopanāhau ca | sirāś cābhīkṣṇaṃ śoṇitamavasecayet
                        || anyatrapāṇḍuśophāditi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.13"><label>4.23.13</label>piṣṭānnamamvlaṃ lavaṇāni
                        madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnamajāṅgalañ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         striyo guḍaṃ tailamatho gurūṇi śophaṃ jighāṃsu parivarjayīta
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.122"><label>4.24.122</label>dṛṣṭyāyustejasāṃ
                        hāniradharmaś ca tato bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         liṅginīṃ gurupatnīñ ca sagotrām atha parvasu | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.123"><label>4.24.123</label>vṛddhāṃ sandhyayoś cāpi
                        garchato jīvitakṣayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         garbhiṇyāṃ garbhapīḍāsyād vyādhitāñ ca valakṣayaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.124"><label>4.24.124</label>hīnāṃgīṃ malināṃ
                        dveṣyāṃ kāmāṃ vandhyām asaṃvṛte |
                        <caesura/>
                         deśe śuddhe ca śukrasya manasaś ca kṣayo bhavet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.125"><label>4.24.125</label>kṣudhitaḥ kṣuvdhacittaś
                        ca madhyāhne tṛṣitovalaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthitāyaṃ hānim āpnoti śukraṃ vāyuś ca kupyati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126"><label>4.24.126</label>vyādhitāyāṃ plīhāmayo
                        mūrcchā doṣaś ca jāyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127"><label>4.24.127</label>pratyūṣe cārdharātre ca
                        vātapittaprakupyataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tiryagyonāv ayonau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128"><label>4.24.128</label>upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ
                        kopaḥ syād retasaḥ kṣayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uccārite mūtrite ca retasaś ca vidhāraṇe |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129"><label>4.24.129</label>uttāne ca bhavec
                        chīghraṃ śukrārśmaryās tu sambhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt sarvaṃ parihared etal lokadvayāhitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130"><label>4.24.130</label>vayor ūpaguṇo py etāṃ
                        kulya kulānvitāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131"><label>4.24.131</label>abhikāmoptikāmāṃś ca
                        hṛṣṭo hṛṣṭām alaṅkṛtāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         seveta pramadān nityaṃ vyājīkaraṇapītavān |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132"><label>4.24.132</label>śarkaropahitāṃ bhakṣyāṃ
                        kṣīrañ cāpi saśarkaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyajanaṃ svapnasevā ca vyavāyānte hitāni tu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133"><label>4.24.133</label>sukhamātraṃ samāsena
                        sadvṛttasyetad īritaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āyur ārogyam artho vā nāsadbhiḥ prāpyate tribhir iti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">❈</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.1"><label>4.25.1</label>athāto miśrikacikitsitaṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.3"><label>4.25.3</label>pālyāmayās tu visrāvyā yaḥ

                        <caesura/>
                         paripoṭas tathotpādovamantho duḥkhavardhanaṃḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.4"><label>4.25.4</label>pañcamaḥ parilehī ca
                        karṇṇapālyāṃ gadāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saukumāryāc cirotsṛṣṭe sahasābhipravardhite |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.5"><label>4.25.5</label>karṇṇaśopho bhavet pālyāṃ
                        sarujaḥ paripoṭavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇāruṇinibhastavdhaḥ savātāt paripoṭakaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.6"><label>4.25.6</label>gurvābharaṇasaṃyogāt
                        tāḍanod gharṣaṇādibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.7"><label>4.25.7</label>rakto vā raktapittābhyām
                        unmādaḥ sa gado mataḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.8"><label>4.25.8</label>sakaphaṃ prāpya kurute
                        śophaṃ stavdhamavedanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.13"><label>4.25.13</label>tasmād āśu bhiṣak teṣu

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.15"><label>4.25.15</label>supiṣṭaiḥ sāśvagandhaiś

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.16"><label>4.25.16</label>sakṣīrāṇyatha taiḥpāliṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.21"><label>4.25.21</label>cūrṇṇair

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.28"><label>4.25.28</label>mṛdvyaḥ puṣṭāḥ samāḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.33"><label>4.25.33</label>kalkānetāṃ

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.35"><label>4.25.35</label>bhavec ca nityaṃ
                        kṛsaropasevī bhuñjīta cānnaṃ māṣayūṣeṇa cāpi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.39"><label>4.25.39</label>suvarṇṇāhvāpāṇḍupatraṃ

                <div n="26" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 26]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.1"><label>4.26.1</label>athātaḥ kṣīṇavalīyaṃ
                        vyājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.3"><label>4.26.3</label>kalasyodagravayaso
                        vyājīkaraṇasevinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣv ṛtuṣv aharahaḥ vyavāyo na nivāritaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.4"><label>4.26.4</label>strīṣv akṣaryyaṃ mṛgayatāṃ
                        vṛddhānāñ ca riraṃsatāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         klīvāṇām alpaśukrāṇāṃ strīṣu kṣīṇāś ca ye narāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.5"><label>4.26.5</label>vilāsinām arthavatāṃ
                        rūpayauvanaśālināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nṛṇām vahvīpatīnāñ ca yogā vyajīkaro hitāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.6"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.7"><label>4.26.7</label>bhojanāni ca citrāṇi pānāni
                        vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vācaḥ srotro nugāminyas tvaksukhasparśanāni ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.8"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.9"><label>4.26.9</label>gandhān manojñaṃ rūpāṇi
                        citrāṇy upavanāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         manasaś cāpratīvāto vyājīkurvanti mānavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tais tair bhāvair ahṛdyais tu riraṃsor manasi kṣate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.10"><label>4.26.10</label>dhvajaḥ pataty adho nṛṇāṃ
                        klaivyaṃ samupajāyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         annair amlvauṣṇalavaṇair atimātropasevitaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.11"><label>4.26.11</label>saumyadhātukṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ
                        klaivyaṃ tad aparaṃ smṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ativyavāyaśīlo vā na ca vyājīkriyārataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.12"><label>4.26.12</label>dhvajabhaṅgam avāpnoti
                        saśukrakṣayahetukaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         meḍhrarogeṇa mahatā marmcachedena vā punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.13"><label>4.26.13</label>klivyaṃ caturtham bhavati
                        nṛṇāṃ puṃstvopaghātajaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.14"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.15"><label>4.26.15</label>asādhyaṃ sahajaṃ klaivyaṃ
                        marmacchedāc ca yad bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyānām avaśiṣṭānāṃ kāryo vyājīkaro vidhiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.16"><label>4.26.16</label>tilamāṣavidārīṇāṃ śālīnāṃ
                        cūrṇṇam eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.17"><label>4.26.17</label>rasair ikṣurasair vāpi
                        marditaṃ saindhavānvita |
                        <caesura/>
                         varāhamedasā yuktaṃ ghṛtenotkārikāṃ pacet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.18"><label>4.26.18</label>tāṃ bhakṣayitvā gaccheyuḥ
                        puruṣaḥ ṣaṣṭhim aṅganāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vastrāṇḍasiddhapayasi bhāvitā na sakṛt tilāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.19"><label>4.26.19</label>śiśumāravasāpakvā tais
                        tilaiḥ śaṣkulīśubhāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaḥ khādet sa pumāṃ gacchet strīṇāṃ śatam apūrvavat ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.20"><label>4.26.20</label>pippalīlavaṇaupetau
                        vastāṇḍau kṣīrasarpiṣi |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhitau bhakṣayed yas tu sa gacchet pramadāśataṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.21"><label>4.26.21</label>māṣapippaliśālīnāṃ
                        yavagodhūmayos tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇabhāgaiḥ samais tais tu ghṛte pūpalikāṃ pacet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.22"><label>4.26.22</label>tāṃ bhakṣayitvā pītvā ca
                        śarkarāmadhuram payaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         naraś caṭakavad gacched daśavārān nirantaraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.23"><label>4.26.23</label>cūrṇṇaṃ vidāryāḥ sakṛtaṃ
                        svarasenaiva bhāvitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥkṣaudrayutaṃ līḍhvā daśanāryodhirohita ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.24"><label>4.26.24</label>evam āmalakaṃ cūrṇṇaṃ
                        svarasenaiva bhāvitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkarāmadhusarpirbhir yuktaṃ līḍhvā payaḥ pivet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.25"><label>4.26.25</label>etenāśītivarṣo pi yuveva
                        parihṛṣyati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīlavaṇaupetau vastāṇḍau ghṛtasādhitau |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.26"><label>4.26.26</label>śiśumārasya vā khādet tau
                        tu vyājīkarau bhṛśaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kulīrakūrmanakrāṇām aṇḍāny evaṃ tu bhakṣayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.27"><label>4.26.27</label>mahiṣarṣabhavastānām
                        pivec chukrāṇi vānaraḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         aśvatthaphalamūlatvaṃ chuṅgasiddham payo 'pi vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.28"><label>4.26.28</label>pītvā saśarkkarākṣaudraṃ
                        kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārīmūlakalkan tu sritena payasā naraḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.29"><label>4.26.29</label>udumvararasam pītvā
                        vṛddho 'pi taruṇāyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         māṣāṇām palam ekan tu saṃyuktam madhusarppiṣā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.30"><label>4.26.30</label>tiṃ līḍhvānupivet kṣīraṃ
                        tena vyājībhavet naraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.31"
                        ><label>4.26.31</label>nakramūṣikamaṇḍūkacaṭakāṇḍakṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.32"><label>4.26.32</label>pādābhyaṅgena kurute
                        vyājībhūmin tu na spṛśet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yāvan na spṛśate bhūmin tāvad gacchen nirantaraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.33"><label>4.26.33</label>svayaṃ guptekṣurakayor
                        vījapūrṇṇaṃ saśarkkaraṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dhāroṣṇena nara payaḥ pītvā payasā na kṣayaṃ vrajet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.34"><label>4.26.34</label>uccaṭācūrṇṇam apy eva
                        kṣīreṇottamam ucyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāvary uccaṭācūrṇṇam payaḥ medo sukhārthinā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svayaṃguptāphalayutaṃ māṣayūṣam pivet naraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.35"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.36"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.37"><label>4.26.37</label>gṛṣṭīnāṃ vṛddhavatsānāṃ
                        māṣacūrṇṇabhṛtāṅgavāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yat kṣīran tat praśansanti balakāmeṣu jantuṣu ||</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         sevyā viśuddhāpacita viśuddhā paricita dehaiḥ kālādy apekṣayeti
                        ||</l>

                <div n="27" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 27 (draft based on MS H)</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.1">
                        <label>4.27.1</label>athātaḥ sarvvāvādhasaṃśamanīyaṃ rasāyanam
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.3">
                        <label>4.27.3</label>pūrvve vayasi madhye vā manuṣyasya rasāyanaṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājñaḥ snigdhaśuddhatanoḥ sadā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.4">
                        <label>4.27.4</label>aviśuddhaśarīrasya yukto rāsāyano vidhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na bhāti vāsasi kliṣṭe raṅgayoga ivāhitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.5">
                        <label>4.27.5</label>śarīrasyopaghātāya doṣajā mānasās tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         upadiṣṭopadeśena teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vāraṇaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.6">
                        <label>4.27.6</label>śītodakam payaḥ kṣaudraṃ ghṛtamekaikaśo
                        dviśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         triśaḥ samastam athavā prāk pītaṃ sthāpayed vayaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.7">
                        <label>4.27.7</label>tatra viḍaṅgataṇḍulam āhṛtya
                        yaṣṭīmadhukamadhuyuktaṃ yathāvalaṃ śītatoyena upayuñjīta śītatoyaṃ
                        cānupivet | aharahar mmāsan tad eva madhuyuktaṃ bhallātakakvāthena
                        | drākṣākvāthena vā madhusaṃyuktaṃ | madhvāmalakarasābhyām vā |
                        guḍūcīkvāthena vā | evam ete pañcaprayogā bhavanti | jīrṇṇe
                        mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇena ghṛtaṃntam odanam aśnīyād iti ghṛtavantam
                        odanam aśnīyāt | etaiḥ khalu durnnāmānaḥ kṣayaṃ yāntikrimayaś
                        copaśāmyanti | grahaṇadhāraṇaśaktiś ca bhavati | māsi māsi ca
                        prayoge varṣaśataṃ varṣaśataṃ āyuṣo 'bhivṛddhir vbhavati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.8">
                        <label>4.27.8</label>viḍaṅgataṇḍuladroṇaṃ
                        piṣṭapavanapiṣṭavadusvedya vigatakaṣāyaṃ susvinnam avatārya dṛśadi
                        prapiṣṭamāyasyāṃ kumbhyāṃ madhūttarodakaṅ kṛtvā | bhasmarāśau
                        prāvṛṣyabhyatarataś ca catu ro māsānnidadhyāt | varṣāvyavāye
                        coddhṛtyopasaṃskṛtaśarīraḥ sahasrasampātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā prātaḥ
                        prātaryathāvalam upayuñjīta | jīrṇṇe mudgayūṣeṇa ghṛtam odanam
                        aśnīyāt | pāṃśuśayyāyāṃ śāyayīta | tasya māsādūrddhaṃ
                        sarvvāṅgebhyaḥ krimayo niḥkrāmanti | tān anutailenābhyaktasya
                        vidalenāpaharet | dvitīye pipīlikās tṛtīye yūkānān tathaivāpaharet
                        | caturthe dantanakharomāṇyavasīryante | pañcame praśasta
                        guṇalakṣaṇāni jāyante | amānuṣañcādityaprakāśam vapuradhigacchati
                        | dūrācchravaṇa darśanāni cāsya bhavati | rajastamasī cāpohya
                        satvamadhitiṣṭhate | śrutanigādī | apūrvvotpādī puṣṭo vṛṣabhavalo
                        'śvajavaḥ punaryuvāṣṭau varṣaśatānyāyuravāpnoti |
                        tasyānutailamabhyaṅgārthe | kaṣāyamājakarṇṇamutsādanārthe |
                        sauśīraṃ kūnūpodakaṃ snānārthe | candanamanulepanārthe |
                        bhallātataka vidhānavadupayogaḥ parihāraś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.9">
                        <label>4.27.9</label>kāśmarīṇānniṣkulīkṛtānāmeṣa eva kalpaḥ |
                        pāṃśuśayyābhojanavarjyaṃ | tatrāpi payasā śritena bhoktavyaṃ |
                        āśiṣaś ca samānāḥ pūrvveṇa | śoṇitapittanimitteṣu vikāreṣveteṣām
                        upayogaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.10">
                        <label>4.27.10</label>yathoktamāgāram praviśya balāmūlārddhapalam
                        palam vā payasyāloḍya pibet | jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity āhāraḥ
                        | evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta tato varṣaśatam vayastiṣṭhati |
                        eṣa eva balātibalānāgabalāvidārīśa tāvarīṇām upayogaḥ | viśeṣatas
                        tu atibalām udakena | nāgabalācūrṇṇaṃ madhukṣīreṇa |
                        śatāvarīmapyevaṃ | pūrvveṇāśiṣaś ca samānāḥ | ete hy
                        auṣadhaprayogāḥ | balakāmānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ raktapittopasṛṣṭānāṃ
                        śoṇitañccharddayatām viricyamānānāñ copadiśyante ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.11">
                        <label>4.27.11</label>vārāhīmūlan tulācūrṇṇaṅ kṛtvā tato mātrām
                        madhuyuktam payasāloḍya pibet | jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity
                        āhāraḥ | prayogam imam upayevamāno varṣaśatam āyur avāpnoti ||
                        strīṣu cākṣayatā | etenaiva cūrṇṇaena
                        payovacūrṇṇāśritaśritaśītam abhimathyājyam utpādya |
                        madhuyuktam upayuñjīta | jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity āhāraḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.12">
                        <label>4.27.12</label>cakṣuḥ kāmaḥ prāṇakāmo vā
                        jīvavījakasārāgnimanthamūlāni kvāthairmmāṣaprasthaṃ sādhayet |
                        tasmin sidhyati citrakamūlānāmakṣamātraṃ kalkan dadyāt |
                        āmalakarasacaturvbhāgan tataḥ susvinnam avatārya śītībhūtam
                        madhusarppirbbhyāṃ saṃsṛjyopayuṃjīta | jīrṇṇe mudgayūṣeṇā lavaṇena
                        ghṛtavantamodanam aśnīyāt | māsamātramevam anena prayogena ca kṣuḥ
                        sauparṇṇam bhavati | alpabalābalāṃ strīṣu cākṣyyo
                        varṣaśatāyurbbhavati || ||</l>

                <div n="30" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 30]</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.1">
                        <label>4.30.1</label><label>4.30.1</label>athāto nivṛttasantāpīyaṃ
                        rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.3">
                        <label>4.30.3</label><label>4.30.3</label>yathā nivṛttasantāpā
                        modantedivi devatāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathauṣadhyastvimāḥ prāpya modante bhuvi mānavāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.4">
                        <label>4.30.4</label><label>4.30.4</label>atha khalu saptavidhāḥ
                        puruṣā rasāyanaṃ nopayuñjīran | tad yathā | anātmavānalaso
                        daridraḥ pramādī vyasanī pāpiṣṭho bheṣajāpamānī ceti || saptabhiḥ
                        kāraṇair na saṃpadyante | tad yathā |
                        ajñānādarambhādasthiracittatvād
                        dāridrādanāyatanādāyāsādauṣadhālābhācceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.5">
                        <label>4.30.5</label><label>4.30.5</label>athauṣadhīn vakṣyāmaḥ |
                        tatrājagarī svetakāpotī gonasī kṛṣṇakāpotī vārāhī cchatrāticchatrā
                        kanyā kareṇu ajā takrakād ity aparṇṇinī vrahmasuvarcalā
                        mahāsrāvaṇī golāmī mahāvegavatī cetyaṣṭādaśa
                        somasamavīryāmahauṣadhayo vyākhyāḥ || tatra tāsāṃ somavat
                        kriyāsīstutatayaḥ śāstrebhihitāḥ | tāsāmagārebhihitānāṃ yāḥ
                        kṣīravatyastāsāṃ kṣīrakuḍavaṃ sakṛdevopuyañjīta |
                        yāstvakṣīrāmūlavatyastāsāṃ pradeśinī pramāṇānī trīṇi kāṇḍāni
                        pramāṇam upayoge | svetakāpotī samūlavṛttā bhakṣayitavyā |
                        gonasyājagarī kṛṣṇakāpotīnāṃ sanakhaṃ muṣṭiṃ kāṇḍasaḥ kalpayitvā
                        kṣīreṇa visrāvya pratisāritamabhighāritamabhihutañ ca
                        sakṛdevopayuñjīta | tatastāsāṃ yānyāpayasā sakṛdeva
                        vrahmasuvarcalā saptarātram upayoktavyā | bhakṣakalpena | śeṣāṇāṃ
                        pañca pañca palāni kṣīrāḍhakakathitāni prasthevaśiṣṭe parisrāvya
                        sakṛdevopayuñjīta | somena cāhāravihārāḥ vyākhyātāḥ | kevalaṃ tu
                        navanītamabhyaṃ gārthe | śeṣaṃ somavadānirgamāditi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.1"><label>4.31.1</label>athātaḥ
                        snehopayogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.3"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.4"
                        ><label>4.31.4</label>dviyoniścaturvikalpobhihitaḥ snehaḥ
                        snehaguṇāś ca | tatra jaṅgamebhyo gavyaṃ snehaṃ pradhāṇatamaṃ
                        sthāvarebhyas tilasneha iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.5"><label>4.31.5</label>ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        yathāprayojanato yathāpradhānataś ca | sthāvarasnehāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ |
                        tatra
                        tilvakairaṇḍakuśāmradantīpalāśaśaṅkhinīviṣāṇigavākṣīkampilyakaśampākanīlinīsnehā
                        virecayanti |. jīmūtakakūṭajakṛtavedhanekṣvākumadanasnehā
                        vāmayanti |. viḍaṅgasthū
                        lamañjarīmadhuśigrusūryavallīpīlusiddhārthakajyotiṣmatīsnehāḥ śiro
                        virecayanti | karañjapūtīkalavaṇamātuluṅgeṅgudīkirātatiktakasnehāḥ
                        duṣṭavraṇeṣūpayojyāḥ |. turuvakakapitthabhallātakapaṭolasnehāḥ
                        mahāvyādhiṣu |. trapusatvārukerkāratumvurukaṣmāṇḍasnehāḥ
                        mūtrasaṅgeṣu ||kapotavaṅkaharītakīsnehāḥ śarkarārśmariṣu |.
                        kusumbhasarṣapātasīpicumardātimuktakakāṇḍīrasnehāḥ prameheṣu |.
                        nāḍīkerapanasapiyālavilvamadhūka śleeṣmātakasnehāḥ pittasaṃsṛṣṭe
                        vāyau || vibhītakapiṇḍītakabhallātakasnehāḥ kṛṣṇīkaraṇeṣu |.
                        śravaṇakaṃgukasnehāḥ pāṇḍūkaraneṣu |
                        saralāpītadāruśiṃśapāsanasārasnehāḥ dardrukiṭibheṣu | sarva eva
                        snehā vātam upahanti | tailaguṇāḥ samāsena vyākhyātāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.6"><label>4.31.6</label>ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        kaṣāyapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra kecidāhus tvak
                        patrapuṣpaphalādīnāṃ bhāgastaccaturguṇamudakaṃ
                        caturthāṃśāvaśeṣitaṃ kvāthyāvatārayed ity eṣa kaṣāyakalpaḥ | tat
                        tu na samyak kasmād āgamasiddhatvāt </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.7"><label>4.31.7</label>palakuḍavādīnām ity etac
                        copadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra dvādaśadhānyamāṣā madhyamā suvarṇṇamāṣakaste
                        śoḍaṣasuvarṇṇāḥ | ataścordhvaṃ caturguṇamabhivardhayataḥ
                        palakuḍavaprasthāḍhakadroṇā abhiniṣpadyante | tulā punaḥ palaśataṃ
                        tābhir viṃśatir bhāraḥ śuṣkāṇām ārdrāṇāṃ dravāṇāṃ ca dviguṇam iti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.8"
                        ><label>4.31.8</label>snehakukuḍavesāṇyakvāthyadravyadurvyaprastho
                        vidheyas taccaturguṇamudakaṃ caturthāṅgāvaśeṣitaṃ kvāthyāvatārayed
                        ity eṣa kaṣāyakalpaḥ | snehakuḍavesāṇya bheṣajapalaṃ kalkam iṣṭaṃ
                        caturguṇañ ca kaṣāyam āvāpya vipaced ity eṣa snehapākakalpa iti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.9"><label>4.31.9</label>bha |. snehabheṣajatoyānāṃ
                        mānaṃ yatra tu neritaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāyaṃ vidhir āstheyo nirdiṣṭe tadvad eva tu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.10"><label>4.31.10</label>anukte dravakārye tu
                        sarvatra salilaṃ smṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkakvāthāvanirdeśe gaṇāt tasmāt samādhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.11"><label>4.31.11</label>ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        snehapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ | sa tu pākas tṛvidho mṛduścikkanaḥ
                        kharacikkaṇa iti | dhavivekamātraṃ yatra bheṣajaṃ sa mṛduḥ |
                        madhūcchiṣṭamivalepayati yatra bheṣajaṃ sa cikkaṇaḥ | phenāni
                        mātra vailasya śeṣaṃ ghṛtavadādiśet kṛṣṇamavasannamīṣadviśadaṃ
                        cikkaṇaṃ ca yatra sa kharacikkaṇa iti |. ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        pradagdhasneha bhavati | taṃ punaḥ sādhayet | tatra pānābhya va
                        nasyābhyañjanīyaś cikkaṇaḥ | vastisnehāḥ kharacikkaṇa iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.12"><label>4.31.12</label>śabdasyoparame prāpte
                        phenasyoparame tathā |.
                        <caesura/>
                         gandhavarṇṇarasānāñ ca sampattau siddham ādiśet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.29"><label>4.31.29</label>glānimūrcchāmadāṃ hitvā

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.30"><label>4.31.30</label>sā tu

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.31"><label>4.31.31</label>pīto hy ativahusneho
                        janayet prāṇasaṃśayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mithyācārādvahutvād vā yasya sneho na jīryati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.32"><label>4.31.32</label>viṣṭabhya vāpi jīryeta
                        vāriṇauṣṇena vāmayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ snehaṃ punardadyāllaghukoṣṭhāya dehine |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīrṇṇājīrṇṇaviśaṃkāyāṃ piveduṣṇodakaṃ naraḥ |</l>
