                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 33]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.1"><label>4.33.1</label>athāto
                        vamanavirecanasādhyopakramacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.3"><label>4.33.3</label>doṣāḥ kṣīṇā bṛṃhayitavyāḥ
                        calitāḥ praśamayitavyāḥ pravṛddhā nirhattavyāḥ svasthānasthārakṣyā
                        iti siddhāntaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.4"><label>4.33.4</label>prādhānyena
                        vamanavirecanenirharaṇe varttate | tasmāt tayor vidhānam ucyamānam
                        upadhārayasva |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.5"><label>4.33.5</label>tad yathāturaṃ
                        snigdhasvinnam anabhiṣyandibhir āhārair anavabaddhadoṣam ālocya
                        svo vamanaṃ pāyayitāsmīti saṃbhojayet | saṃbhojyas tu tīkṣṇāgnir
                        balavān bahudoṣo mahāvyādhiparigṛhīto vamanasātmyaś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.6"><label>4.33.6</label>peśalair vividhairannair
                        doṣamutkliśya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnāya vamanaṃ dattaṃ samyak pravarttate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.7"><label>4.33.7</label>athāparedyuḥ pūrvāhṇe
                        sādhāraṇe kāle vamanadravyakaṣāyakalkacūrṇṇasnehanānyatamasya
                        mātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet | asātmyabībhatsadudarśanadurgandhāni
                        vāmanīyāni vidadhyād ato viparītāni |. tatra sukumārāṃ kṛśaṃ bālaṃ
                        vṛddhāṃ bhīrum vā vamanasādhyavikāreṣu
                        kṣīradadhitakrayavāgūnāmanyatamamākaṇṭhaṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        pītauṣadhañcapāṇibhir agnitaptair upaspṛśyamānaṃ muhūrttam
                        upekṣeta | tatra pravṛttahṛllāsaṃ jñātvā jānumātrāsanopaviṣṭam
                        anyena hṛtpṛṣṭhayoḥ pāṇibhyāṃ uparigṛhītam
                        aṅguligandharvahastapatravṛttotpalanālānām anyatamena
                        kaṇṭhamanabhis pṛśan vāmayet yāvat samyag vāntalakṣaṇāni bhavanti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.8"><label>4.33.8</label>kaphaprasekaṃ
                        hṛdayāviśuddhiṃ kaṇḍūñ ca duścharditaliṅgam āhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittātiyogañ ca visaṅjñatāñ ca hṛtkaṇṭhapīḍām api cātivānte |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.9"><label>4.33.9</label>pitte kaphasyāndramukhaṃ
                        pravṛtte śuddheṣu hṛtkaṇṭhaśirassu cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghau ca dehe kaphasaṃsrave ca sthite suvāntaṃ puruṣaṃ
                        vyavavasyet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.10"><label>4.33.10</label>samyagvāntaṃ cainam abhis
                        amīkṣya snaihikavairecanikopaśamanīyānāṃ dhūmānām anyataṃ
                        sāmarthyataḥ pāyayitvā cārikam upadiśet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.11"><label>4.33.11</label>tato parāhṇe
                        suvibhaktadeham uṣṇābhir ahniḥ pariṣiktagātraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kulattham udgaḍhakijāṅgalānāṃ yuṣai rasair vāpy upabhojayīta
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.12"><label>4.33.12</label>kaphaprasekaḥ
                        svarabhedatandrā nidrāsyadaurgandhyaviṣopasargāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurutvakaṇḍūgrahaṇīpradoṣā na santijantorvamataḥ kadācit |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.13"><label>4.33.13</label>chinne tarau
                        puṣpaphalaprarohā yathāvināśaṃ sahasā vrajanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathāhṛte śleṣmaṇi ccharddanena tajjā vikārā vilayaṃ vrajanti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.14"><label>4.33.14</label>na vāmayet
                        taimirikannagulminaṃ na caivapāṇḍūdararogapīḍitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlakṣatakṣīṇakṛśātivṛddhā narśorditā kṣepakapīḍitāṃś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.15"><label>4.33.15</label>rūkṣaṃ pramehe taraṇe ca
                        garbhe gacchatyadhordhvaṃ rudhire ca tīvre |
                        <caesura/>
                         tuṣṭe ca koṣṭhe krimibhir manuṣyaṃ na vāmayed varcasi cātivṛddhe
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.16"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.17"><label>4.33.17</label>ete py ajīrṇṇavyathitā
                        vāmyā ye ca viṣāturāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atīvacolbaṇakaphās te ca syur madhukāmbunā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.18"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.19"><label>4.33.19</label>virecanam api
                        snigdhasvinnāya ca deyaṃ | avāntasya hi samyagviriktasyāpi
                        satovasrastaḥ śleṣmāgra haṇīñ chādayati | gauravam āpādayati
                        pravāhikām vā kurute | tasmāt snigdhasvinnāya vāntāya ca deyam
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.20"><label>4.33.20</label>athāturaṃ svo virecanaṃ
                        pāyayitāsmīti pūrvāhṇe laghubhojayet |
                        phalāmvlamuṣṇodakaścainamanupāyayet | athāparehani
                        vigataśleṣmadhātāvāt uropakramaṇīyād apekṣyāturam athāsmai
                        virecanaṃ mātrāṃ prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.21"><label>4.33.21</label>tatra mṛduḥ krūro madhya
                        iti trividhaḥ koṣṭho bhavati | tatra bahupitto mṛduḥ sa dugdhenā
                        viricyate | bahuvātaśleṣmā krūro durvirecyaḥ | sagadoṣo madhyaḥ
                        sādhāraṇa iti | tatra mṛdau mṛdvī mātrā | tīkṣṇakrūre | madhye
                        madhyā karttavyeti | pītauṣadhaś ca tanmanāḥ śayyābhyāse viricyeta
                        | na prāptavegaṃ vidhārayet | na cāprāptaṃ prāṇenākāṃkṣeta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.22"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.23"><label>4.33.23</label>yathā ca vamane krameṇa
                        prasekauṣadhaḥ pittānilāgacchanty evaṃ virecane
                        vātamūtrapurīṣapittakaphā iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.24"><label>4.33.24</label>bha ||hṛtkukṣyaśuddhiḥ
                        paridāhakaṇḍūviṇmūtrasaṃgaś ca na sadvirikte |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchāgudabhraṃśakaphātiyogāḥ śūlodgamāś cātiviriktaliṅgaṃ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.25"><label>4.33.25</label>gateṣu doṣeṣu
                        kaphāntakeṣu glānyelaghutve manasaś ca tuṣṭau |
                        <caesura/>
                         gatenile cāpy anulomabhāvaṃ samyagviriktaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavasyet
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.26"
                        ><label>4.33.26</label>mandāgnimakṣīṇamasadviriktaṃ na pāyayet tad
                        divasaṃ yavāgūṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaṃ tṛṣārttaṃ suvirecitaś ca tanvī sukhoṣṇaṃ laghu pāyayīta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.27"><label>4.33.27</label>buddheḥ prasādaṃ
                        balamindriyāṇāṃ dhātusthiratvaṃ jvalanābhivṛddhiṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti virecanaṃ samyagupāsyamānaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.28"><label>4.33.28</label>yathodakānāṃ tu
                        vijaṅgamānāṃ rodhevadīrṇṇe dhruva eva nāśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte hṛtendhevam upadravāṇāṃ pittātmikākānāṃ vihito vināśaḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.29"
                        ><label>4.33.29</label>kṣīṇāḥkṛśārūkṣitabālavṛddhādīnotha śoṣī
                        bhayaśokataptaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śāntas tṛṣārtto parijīrṇṇabhakto garbhiṇyadho gacchati yasya
                        cāsṛk |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.30"><label>4.33.30</label>navapratiśyāyaparītadeho
                        navajvarīyā ca navaprasūtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyan ity āna virecanīyā snehādibhir ye tv anupaskṛtāś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.31"
                        ><label>4.33.31</label>atyarthapittābhiparītadehāṃ virecayet tān
                        api mandamandaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanair yāṃti narā vināśam ajñaprayuktair avirecanīyā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.32"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.33"
                        ><label>4.33.33</label>saratvasaukṣmyataikṣṇyoṣṇe vikāśitvād
                        virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vamanaṃ tu hareddoṣāṃ samyaguktaṃ vṛthānyathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.34"><label>4.33.34</label>mādāya pyamānaṃ virecanaṃ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇodrekād vrajedūrdhvam apakvaṃ vamanaṃ punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.35"><label>4.33.35</label>mṛdukoṣṭhasya dīptāgner
                        dattaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na samyag nirhared doṣān ativegapradhāvitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.36" met="hypermetrical"><label>4.33.36"
                            met="hypermetrical</label>prātar yad auṣadhaṃ pītaṃ
                        bhaktapākasame kṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         paktaṃ gacchati doṣāṃs tu nirharen niravaśeṣataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.37"><label>4.33.37</label>durvalasya naḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         haret prabhūtānalpāṃs tu samayet pracyutānatha |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.38"><label>4.33.38</label>hareddoṣāṃ calān pakvaṃ
                        balino durbalasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         calā hy upekṣitā doṣāḥ kleśayeyuś ciran naraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.39"><label>4.33.39</label>mandāgniṃ krūrakoṣṭhañ ca
                        sakṣāralavaṇairghṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sandhukṣitāgni snigdhañ ca svinnañcaiva viśodhayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.40"><label>4.33.40</label>snigdhasvinnasya
                        bhaiṣajyair doṣas tu kleśito bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cālīyeta mārgeṣu snigdhe bhāṇḍa ivodakaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.41"><label>4.33.41</label>na cātisnigdhakāyāya
                        dadyāt snerhavirecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ pracyāvitā bhūyo līyante tena vartmasu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.42"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.43"><label>4.33.43</label>virūkṣya snehasātmyantu
                        bhūyaḥ saṃsnehya recayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tena doṣā hṛtās tasya bhavanti snehabandhanāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.44"><label>4.33.44</label>prāgadhītauṣadhaṃ śodhya
                        pāyayet mṛduśodhaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato vijñātakoṣṭhasya kāryaṃ saṃśodhaṇaṃ punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.45"><label>4.33.45</label>sukhaṃ dṛḍhaphalaṃ hṛdyam
                        alpamātraṃ mahāguṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāpat svalpātyayañ cāpi piben nṛpatir auṣadhaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.46"><label>4.33.46</label>snehasvedāvakṛtvāgre yas
                        tu saṃśodhanaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāru śuṣkamivānāme dehas tasya viśīryate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.47"><label>4.33.47</label>snehasvedapracalito
                        rasaiḥ snigdhair udīritā |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ koṣṭhagatā jantoḥ sukhaṃ hartuṃ virecanair iti ||</l>

                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 34 (draft based on MS H)</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.1">
                        <label>4.34.1</label>athāto vamanavirekavyāpaccikitsitam
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.3">
                        <label>4.34.3</label>vaidyāturanimittam vamanam virecanañ ca ||
                        pañcadaśadhā vyāpadyate tatra vamanasyādho gacchaty ūrddhvam
                        virecanasya | sāmānyam ubhayoḥ sāvaśeṣauṣadhatvam alpadoṣahṛtatvaṃ
                        jīrṇṇauṣadham vātaśūlam ayogātiyogau jīvādānamādhmānam parikarttaḥ
                        parisrāvaḥ pravāhikā hṛdayasaraṇa vibandha iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.4">
                        <label>4.34.4</label>tatra bubhukṣāpīḍitasya tīkṣṇāgner
                        mmṛdukoṣṭhasya vāvatiṣṭhamānaṃ durvvāntasya vā guṇasāmānyād
                        vamanam adho gacchati | tatrepsitān avāptir ddoṣo kleśaś ca tam
                        āśusnehayitvā bhūyastīkṣṇatarair vvāmayet iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.5">
                        <label>4.34.5</label>apariśuddhāmāśayasyotkliṣṭaśleṣmaṇaḥ
                        sāvaśeṣān nasya vā'hṛdyam bahudhāvacāritam vā virecanam ūrddham
                        tiṣṭhati tatrepsitān avāptibastidoṣān kleśatamulbaṇaśleṣmāṇamāśu
                        || 1|| vāmayitvā bhūyas tīkṣṇatarair vvirecayet iti | āmāśaye
                        tvāmavat samvidhānaṃ | ahṛdyetiprabhūte ca hṛdyam pramāṇayuktañ ca
                        | tathā tathāpy uttiṣṭhati tṛtīye nna pāyayet ataś cainam
                        madhughṛtaphāṇitayuktairllehayitvā virecayet iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.6">
                        <label>4.34.6</label>doṣavigrathitamalpamauṣadham
                        avasthitamūrddhabhāgikam adhobhāgikam vā na sraṃsayatidoṣān |
                        tatra
                        tṛṣṇāpārśvaśūlañccharddimūrcchāparvvabhedohṛllāsorucirudgarāviśuddhiś
                        ca bhavati | tam uṣṇābhir adbhir āśu vāmayet | ūrddhvabhāgikam
                        adhobhāgikam vā sāvaśeṣauṣadham apradhāvitadoṣam atibalamasamyag
                        viriktalakṣaṇam upayuktam alpam apy evam vāmayet iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.7">
                        <label>4.34.7</label>krūrakoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇāgner alpamapyauṣadham
                        alpaguṇam vā bhaktavat pākam upaiti | tatra samudīrṇṇa doṣāḥ |
                        yathākālam anirhriyamāṇā vibhramaṃ kurvvanti |
                        tamanalpamamandañcauṣadham pāyayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.8">
                        <label>4.34.8</label>snigdhasvinnenālpam alpaguṇam vā bheṣajam
                        upayuktam alpān doṣān harati | taddoṣaśeṣam vamanagauravam
                        upakleśa hṛdayāṃ viśuddhiṃ vyādhivivṛddhiñ ca karoti roga)| tatra
                        yathāyogam pāyayitvā vāmayed dṛḍhataraṃ | virecanadoṣaśeṣaṃ
                        gudaparikarttam ādhmānaṃ gauravamanisaraṇam vāyor vvyādhivivṛddhiñ
                        ca karoti | tam upapādya snehasvedābhyāṃ bhūyo virecayed
                        dṛḍhataraṃ | dṛḍhaṃ pracalitadoṣam vā tṛtīye divasa iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.9">
                        <label>4.34.9</label>asnigdhasvinne rūkṣamauṣadham
                        upayuktamabrahmacāriṇā vā vāyuṃ kopayati | tatra vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ
                        pārśvapṛṣṭhaśoṇitamanyāmarmma muśūlaṃ mūrcchā bhrama saṃjñānāśañ
                        ca karoti | tadvātaśūlam ity ācakṣate | tamabhyajya dhānyasvedena
                        svedayitvā yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tailenānu vā vāmayed iti pāṭhaḥ
                        |sayati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.10">
                        <label>4.34.10</label>snehasvedābhyām avibhāvita
                        śarīreṇauṣadhamalpaguṇam vā pītamūrddhamadho vā nābhyeti
                        doṣām̐ścopakleśya taiḥ saha balakṣayamāpādayati | tatrādhmānaṃ
                        hṛdayagrahastṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhaś ca bhavati | tam ayogam ity ācakṣate
                        |tam āśu vāmayed virecayed vā durvvāntasya tu samutkliṣṭā doṣāḥ |
                        vyāpyaśarīraṃ kaṇḍūśvayathukoṭhapiṭakajvarāṅgasādanāni kurvvanti
                        tatas tān aśeṣān sahauṣadhenāpaharet | durvviriktasya tu
                        stabdhapūrṇṇodaratā bastiśūlomeḍhratodo vātamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaśaḥ
                        kaṇḍūrmaṇḍalaprādurbbhāvaś ca bhavati | tamāsthapya punaḥ
                        snehayitvā virecayet tīkṣṇeneti | nātipravarttamāne tiṣṭhati vā
                        duṣṭasaṃśodhane tatsantejanārtham uṣṇodakam pāyayet | pāṇitāpaiś
                        ca pārśvodaram upasvedayet tataḥ pravarttate doṣāḥ | anupravṛtte
                        'lpe doṣe jīrṇṇecauṣadhe ca bahudoṣam antaḥ śailam balañ cāvekṣya
                        bhūyo mātrāṃ<del>ñ ca</del> vidadhyād anupravṛtta bhenyūbhaṃ vā
                        daśajātrādūrddham upasthitadehaṃ bhūyaḥ śodhayed
                        durvviriktamāsthāpya punaḥ snehayitvā virecayet | hrībhayalobhaiś
                        ca vegāghātaśīlāḥ prāyaśaḥstriyo rājasamīpasthā vaṇijaḥ śrotriyāś
                        ca bhavanti | tasmād etair ddurvvirecyāḥ | bahuvātatvāt |
                        ataścaināṃ susvinnasnigdhān virecayed iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.11">
                        <label>4.34.11</label>snigdhasvinnasyātimātramatimṛdukoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇamadhikam
                        vābheṣajamatiyogaṅ kuryāt | tatra vamanātiyoge pittātipravṛttir
                        bbalavisraṃso vātakopo balavām̐ś ca bhavati | tamabhyajyāvagāhya
                        ca śītā svapsu śītaiḥ śarkkarāmiśrair llehair upacared iti |
                        virecanātiyoge kaphātipravṛttiruttarakālañ ca saraktasya tatrāpi
                        balavisraṃsā vātakopo balavām̐ś ca bhavati | tamabhyajya śītābhir
                        adbhiḥ pariṣicyāvagāhya śītais taṇḍulāmbubhir mmadhumiśrair
                        vvāmayet | picchābastiñcāsmai dadyāt | kṣīrarasayoścainam
                        anyatamena bhojayet kṣīrasarppiṣā cainam anuvāsayet |
                        priyaṅgvādiñcāsmai taṇḍulāmbunā pātum prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.12">
                        <label>4.34.12</label>tasmin eva ca vamanotiyoge tipravṛtte
                        śoṇitaṃ ṣṭhīvati ccharddayati vā raktaṃ tatra jihvāniḥsaraṇam
                        avasarppaṇañ cākṣṇor vvyāvṛttihanusaṃhananaṃ tṛṣṇā hikkāṅgarau
                        visaṃ jñatvam ity upadravā bhavanti | tam
                        ativisrutaśoṇitavidhānena nopacaret |
                        jihvānniḥsarppitāntrikaṭukalavaṇacūrṇṇapraghṛṣṭāmantaḥ pīḍayet
                        praviṣṭāyām anyemlamasya purastāt khādeyuḥ | vyāvṛtte cākṣiṇī
                        ghṛtābhyaktaiḥ pīḍayet | hanusaṃhanane vātaśleṣmaharan nasyaṃ
                        svedañ ca vidadhyāt | tṛṣṇādiṣu ca yathāsvaṃpratikurvvīta |
                        visaṃjñam vā veṇuvīṇāgītasvenaṃ srāvayed iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.13">
                        <label>4.34.13</label>virecanātiyoge sacandrakaṃsalilam adhaḥ
                        sravati tato māṃsadhāvanaprakāśamuttarakālaṃ jīvaśoṇitañ ca |
                        tatra gudaniḥsaraṇaṃ vepathur vvamanātiyogopadravāś ca bhavanti |
                        tam atisrutavidhānenaivopacaret | niḥsarppitaṅ gudam abhyajya
                        parisvedyān pīḍayet | kṣudrarogacikitsite gudasraṃsacikitsitañ
                        cāvekṣyeta | vepathau vātavyādhividhānaṅ kurvvīta |
                        jihvāniḥsarppaṇādiṣūktaḥ pratīkāraḥ | atipravṛtte vā
                        nyagrodhādikaṣā yakṣīrekṣurasaghṛtasaṃsṛṣṭaiścainaṃ bastir
                        upācaret |śoṇitaniṣṭhīvane raktātisāraraktapittakriyāś cānyasya
                        vidadhyān nyagrodhādiñcāsyapānabhojaneṣūpayuñjīta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.14">
                        <label>4.34.14</label>jīvaśoṇitaraktapittayo jijñāsārtham picu
                        plotam vātra prakṣipet tad uṣṇodakaprakṣālitam avarajyeta taj
                        jīvaśoṇita m ity avagantavyam amṛgbhoktum vā śune dadyāt sa yady
                        upayuñjyāt taj jīvaśoṇitam ity avagantavyam iti | tayoś ca
                        raktipittātīsārakriyām vidadhīta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.15">
                        <label>4.34.15</label>sa śeṣānnenānilaprāyakoṣṭhenāsnigdhena vā
                        pītamauṣadham ādhmāpayati | tatrānilamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaḥ |
                        samunnaddhodaratā pārśvabhaṅgo gudabastitudanañ ca bhavati |
                        tamādhmānam ity ācakṣate | tam upasvedyānāha
                        varttidīpanabastikriyābhir yojyā iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.16">
                        <label>4.34.16</label>kṣāmeṇātimṛdukoṣṭhena tīkṣṇamatyuṣṇam
                        atilavaṇ atirūkṣam vā bheṣajam upayuktam pittānilau pradūṣya
                        nātibastigudaparikarttanam āpādayati | tām parikarttiketyācakṣate
                        || taṃ yaṣṭīmadhukakṛṣṇatilamadhughṛtayuktaiḥ picchābastibhir
                        āsthāpayet | śītāmbupariṣiktañcainaṃ payasā bhuktavantaṃ ghṛtam
                        aṇḍanayaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena vā tailenānuvāsayed iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.17">
                        <label>4.34.17</label>krūrakoṣṭhasyātiprabhūtadoṣasya vā
                        mṛdvalpamauṣadhamavacāritaṃ samutkleśya doṣānna niḥśeṣān apaharati
                        | pākañcopaiti | tatra daurbbalyodaraviṣṭambhārucirggātrasadanāni
                        bhavanti | sa vedanau cāsyapittaśleṣmāṇau sravatas tam parisrāvam
                        iti ācakṣate | tamajakarṇṇadhavatiniśa palāsakaṣāyair
                        mmadhuyuktair āsthāpayet | upaśāntadoṣam bhūyaḥ saṃśodhayed</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.18">
                        <label>4.34.18</label>atirūkṣetisnigdhe vā bheṣajam avacāritam
                        aprāptaṃ purīṣam udīrayato vigevighātena pravāhikā bhavati | tatra
                        sadāha śūlaṃ svetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ raktam vā bhṛśaṃ pravāhamāṇaḥ kapham
                        upaviśati | tam pratisrāvavidhānenopacaret</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.19">
                        <label>4.34.19</label>yastūrddhamadhovā bheṣajaṃ
                        vegapravṛttamajñānād vinihanti tasyopasaraṇaṃ hṛdi kurvvanti doṣas
                        tatra pradhānamarmmasantāpād vedanābhir atyartham pīḍyamādantāṃ
                        kaṭakaṭāyatyudvṛttākṣo jihvāṃ khādati pratāmyamānacetā ca bhavati
                        | tamabhyajya dhānasvedena svedayitvā tīkṣṇena dviśiro
                        virecanenopacared yaṣṭīmadhukamiśreṇa cainan taṇḍulāmbunā vāmayed
                        yathā doṣaguṇocchreyaścainam bastibhir upācared iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.20">
                        <label>4.34.20</label>yastūrddhamadhovā pravṛttadoṣaḥ śītāṅgāram
                        udakam anilam anyad vā seveta tasya doṣāḥ srotaḥ svavalīyamānā
                        ghanībhāvam āpannā vātamūtrapurīṣagrahamāpādya vibadhyante ||
                        tasyāṭopo jvaro dāho vedanā ca tīvrā bhavati | tamāśu vāmayitvā
                        prāptayitvā prāptakālaṃ kriyāṃ yojayed iti || adho
                        bhāgetvabhāgaharadravye saindhavāmlalavaṇa mūtrasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ pāyayed
                        āsthāpanamanuvāsanañ ca yathādoṣam vidadhyād yathādoṣamāhārakramaś
                        ca | ūrddhvabhāge tu upadravaviśeṣāt yathāsvaṃ pratikurvvīta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.21">
                        <label>4.34.21</label>yā tu virecane gudaparikīrttitā tad vamāne
                        kañcakaṣaṇaṃ yadadhaḥ parisravaṇaṃ sa ūrddhaṅ kaphaprasekaḥ | yā
                        tvadhaḥ pravāhikā sa ūrddhaṅ śuṣkoṅkādgāra iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.22">

                        tatvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etā virekāti yogā duryogā yogajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">|| cikitsā lahya ||</p>

                        <label>4.35.3</label>atra snehādīnāṅkarmmaṇām
                        bastikarmmapradhānatamam ācakṣate | kasmād anekakarmmaprakāratvāt
                        | ba stirihakhalu nānāvidhadravyasaṃyogād doṣāṇāṃ saṃśodhanaṃ
                        saṃśamanasaṅgrahaṇāni karoti | kṣīṇam vyājīkaroti | kṛśaṃ
                        bṛṃhayati | sthūlaṃ karṣayati | cakṣuḥ prīṇayati | balīpalitam
                        upahanti | vayaḥ sthāpayati iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.4">

                        <caesura/>
                         parivṛddhiñ ca karoti basti samyagupāsitāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.5">
                        <label>4.35.5</label>tathā
                        jvarātīsāratimirapratiśyāyaśirorogādhimanthārdditā

                        ddhyupadaṃśānāhamūtrakṛcchragulmavātaśoṇitavātamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaśukrodāvarttaśukrārttabastanyanāśahṛddhanumanyāgrahaṇaśarkkarāśmarimūḍhagarbbhaprabhṛtiṣu
                        ca vikāreṣv atyartham upayujyata iti ||</l>

                        pūryate |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.7">

                        agreṅgulādhyarddhāṅguladhyarddhāṅgulatryaṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇṇikāni
                            śyenabarhikaṅka<del>gṛdhra</del>patranāḍītulya praveśānāni

                        cāsthāpanadravyapramāṇamāturahastasammitausanmiśrau prasṛtau dvau
                        catvārāṣṭau vidheyā |</l>

                <div n="36" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 36 (draft based on MS H)</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.1">
                        <label>4.36.1</label>athāto netrabastivyāpaccikitsitam
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.2.1">
                        <label>4.36.2.1</label>tatra netrañ calitam vivarttitam
                        pārśvāvapīḍitam atyuttkṣiptam avasannan tiryakkṣiptam iti
                        ṣaghraṇidhānadoṣāḥ | atisthūlaṅ karkkaśāgram avanatam
                        anubhinnasannikṛṣṭakarṇṇikaṃ śūkṣmātimajacchidram alpam atidīrgham
                        atihrasvam ity ekādaśanetradoṣāḥ || bahalatālpatā cchidratā
                        prastdhānatā durbbaladurbbaddheti tveti pañca bastidoṣāḥ |
                        atipīḍitatā śithilapīḍitatā bhūyo vapīḍitatā kālātikramateti
                        catvāraḥ pīḍanadoṣāḥ | āmaṃ hīnam atimātram atiśītam atyuṣṇam
                        atitīkṣṇaṇ ativṛddham atisnigdham atirūkṣm atisāndram atidravam
                        ity ekādaśadravyadoṣāḥ | avāṅcīrṣo cchīrṣony
                        ubjauttānasaṅkucitotthitasatthitādadakṣiṇapārśvaśāyinam
                        avanatapratānam ity aṣṭau śayyādoṣāḥ | evam etāḥ pañcacatvāriṃśad
                        vyāpado vaidyanimattā bhavanti |āturanimittās tu pañcadaśa
                        āturopadravīye vakṣyante | snehastvaṣṭābhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ praṇihito na
                        pratyāgacchati | tad yathā tribhir doṣai rasanābhibhūto
                        malavyāmiśro dūrānupraviṣṭo svinnasyānuṣṇolpaṃ bhuktavato lpāṃśaś
                        cetyetāḥ | vaidyāturanimittā bhavanti | ubhayor bbastyor ayogaḥ |
                        ādhmānaṃ parikarttaḥ parisrāvaḥpravāhikā hṛdayopasaraṇam
                        aṅgapragraho tiyogo jīvādānam ity etān avavyāpado vaidyanimittā
                        eva bhavanti || ṣaṭsaptabhiḥ samāsena vyāpadaḥ parikīrttitāḥ
                        |tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vijñānaṃ siddhiñ ca tadanantaraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.3">

                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tīkṣṇataro bastir hitañ cāpy anuvāsanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.36">
                        <label>4.36.36</label>atitīkṣṇoṣṇalavaṇo rūkṣo bastiḥ prayojitaḥ
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sapittaṃ kopayed vāyuṅ kuryāt saparikarttikān |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.37">
                        <label>4.36.37</label>nābhibastir ggudan tatra kṛtyanta iti
                        dehinaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastir hitas tatra snehaś ca madhuraiḥ śritaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.38">
                        <label>4.36.38</label>atyuṣṇatīkṣṇalavaṇaḥ parisrāvāya kalpate |
                        <caesura/>
                         daurbbalyam aṅgasādañ ca jāyate tatra dehinaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.39">
                        <label>4.36.39</label>parisravatyadhaḥ pittaṃ dāhaḥ sañjanayed
                        gude ||
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastir hitas tatra bastiḥ kṣīraghṛtasya ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.40">
                        <label>4.36.40</label>pravāhikā bhavettīkṣṇā nirūhāt sānuvāsanāt
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sadāhaśūlaṃṃ kṛcchreṇa kaphantatropaveśyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.41">
                        <label>4.36.41</label>picchābastir hitas tatra payasā caiva
                        bhojanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarppir madhukasiddhañ ca tailam vāpy anuvāsanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.42">
                        <label>4.36.42</label>atitīkṣṇo nirūho vā satatam vānuvāsanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdayasyopasaraṇaṃ kurute 'thāṅgasādanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.43">
                        <label>4.36.43</label>doṣais tatra rujāstīvrā mado mūrcchāṃ
                        sagauravaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvadoṣaharaṃ bastiṃ śodhanaṃ tatra dāpayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.44">
                        <label>4.36.44</label>rūkṣasya bahuvātasya syād duḥkhaṃ śayitasya
                        vā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bastipragraham aṅgānāṃ kuryād rukṣo lpabheṣajāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.45">
                        <label>4.36.45</label>tatrāṅgasādaprastambha jṛmbhodveṣṭanavepakāḥ
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvabhedaś ca tatreṣṭāḥ svedābhyañjanabastayaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.46">
                        <label>4.36.46</label>atyuṣṇatīkṣṇo 'tibahur ddattātisveditasya vā
                        ||
                        <caesura/>
                         alpadoṣasya vā bastir atiyogāya kalpate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.47">
                        <label>4.36.47</label>virecanātiyogena samānan tatra lakṣaṇaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastiḥ samābhyāsa<del>ḥ</del>s tasya śītaḥ sukhāvahaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.48">
                        <label>4.36.48</label>atiyogāt paraṃ hanti jīvādānam viriktavat ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dehaṃ deyāṃs tatra hitānāhuḥ picchābastiṃ saśoṇitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.49"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.50"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.51">
                        <label>4.36.51</label>pakṣād vireko vāntasya nirūhahyaś
                        cānuvāsitaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sadyo niruho 'nuvāsasya saptarātrād virecita iti ||</l>

                        savyam prasārayet sakthi dakṣiṇaṃ cāpasaṃharet | madhyāhne

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.1"><label>4.39.1</label> athāta
                        āturopadravakitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.3"><label>4.39.3</label> snehapīsya vāntasya
                        viriktasyāśrutāsṛjaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirūḍhasya ca kāyāgnir mando bhavati dehinaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.4"><label>4.39.4</label> so nnair atyarthagurubhir
                        upayuktaiḥ praśāmyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         alpo mahadbhir bahudhā chādite gnir ivendhanaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.5"><label>4.39.5</label> sa cālpair laghubhiś
                        cānnair upayuktair vivardhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāṣṭhair aṇubhir alpaiś ca sandhukṣita ivānalaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.6"><label>4.39.6</label> hṛtadoṣapramāṇena sa
                        cāhāravidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trīṇi cātra pramāṇāni prastho rdhāḍhakam āḍhakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.7"><label>4.39.7</label> tatrāvaraṃ prasthamātraṃ
                        dve śeṣe madhyamottame |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasthe tv eke gate deyā yavāgūsvalpatāṇḍulā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.8"><label>4.39.8</label> dve caivārdhāḍhake deye
                        tisraś cāpy āḍhake gate |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.9"> dadyāt klinnan tataḥ paścāt mudgayūṣeṇa
                        bhojanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tribhāgakalitaṃ samyag akṛtenārddhasammitaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.25"><label>4.39.25</label> krudhyataḥ kupitaḥ

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.26"><label>4.39.26</label> maithunopagamād ghorāṃ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.27"><label>4.39.27</label> guhyapradeśe śvayathuṃ
                        kāśaśvāsau ca dāruṇau |
                        <caesura/>
                         śukravac cāsya rudhiraṃ sarujaṃ sampravarttate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.28"><label>4.39.28</label> divāsvapnāt tu labhate
                        tāṃs tā vyādhīn kaphātmakāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratiśyāyaṃ jvaraṃ śophaṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ plihodaraṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.29"><label>4.39.29</label> mohaṃ sadanam aṅgānāṃ
                        sāvipākam arocakaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tamasā cābhibhūtaś ca svapnam evābhinandati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.30"><label>4.39.30</label> uccaiḥ sambhāṣaṇād vāyuḥ
                        śirasy āpādayed rujaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āndhyam vādhiryamaghratvaṃ mūkatā jaḍatām api | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.31a"><label>4.39.31a</label> arditaṃ sahanum mokṣam
                        adhīmantha dāruṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.31b"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.32"><label>4.39.32</label> labhate dantacālañ ca
                        tāṃs tāṃś cānyān upadravān |
                        <caesura/>
                         yānayānāt tu labhate cchardiṃ mūrcchā bhramaṃ klamaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.33"><label>4.39.33</label> tathāṅgapragrahaṃ ghoram
                        indriyāṇāñ ca vibhramaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cirāsanāt tathā sthānāc chroṇyāṃ bhavati vedanā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.34"><label>4.39.34</label> aticaṅkramaṇād vāyur
                        jaṃghorvvoḥ kurute rujaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakthnoḥ praśoṣaṃ śopham vā pādaharṣam athāpi vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35a"><label>4.39.35a</label> śītasambhogatoyānāṃ
                        sevā mārutavṛddhaye |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35b"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.36"><label>4.39.36</label> vātātapābhyām vaivarṇyaṃ
                        jvaraṃ vāpi nigacchati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         viruddhādhyaśanān mṛtyuṃ vyādhiṃ vā ghoram arcchati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.37"><label>4.39.37</label> asātmyabhojanād dhanyād
                        balavarṇṇāvasaṃśayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anātmavantaḥ paśuvad bhuṃjate ye pramāṇataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogānīkasya te mūlam ajīrṇṇāt prāpnuvanti haḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.38"><label>4.39.38</label> vyāpadāṃ kāraṇaṃ vīkṣya
                        vyāpatsv eteṣu buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayatetāturārogyai pratyanīkena hetunā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.39"><label>4.39.39</label> viriktavāntair
                        hariṇaiṇalāvakāḥ śaśāś ca sevyāḥ samayūratittirāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṣaṣṭikāś cāpi purāṇaśālayas tathaiva mudgā laghu yac ca
                        kīrttitam iti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer"> || ci 39 || ❈ || </p>

                    <head>[Adhyāya 40]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.1"><label>4.40.1</label> athāto dhūmanastaḥ
                        kavalacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.3"><label>4.40.3</label> pañcavidho dhūmo bhavati |
                        tad yathā | prāyogikaḥ snaihiko vairecanikaḥ kāsaghno vāmanīya iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.4"><label>4.40.4</label> tatrailādinā
                        kuṣṭhatagaravarjyena ślakṣṇapiṣṭena dvādaśāṅgulaṃ śarakāṇḍaṃ
                        daśāṅgulagarbham aṅgula m aṅguṣṭhodara pariṇāhaṃ kṣaumeṇāṣṭāṅgulam
                        pariveṣṭyālepayed eṣā varttiḥ prāyogikaḥ ||
                        snehaphalasāramadhūcchiṣṭasarjarasagugguluprabhṛtibhiś ca
                        snehamiśraiḥ snaihikaiḥ || śirovirecanadravyair vairecanikaiḥ ||
                        bṛhatīkaṇṭakārikātrikaṭukakāsamardahiṃgviṅgudītvaṅmanaḥśilācchinnaruhākarkaṭakasṛṅgīprabhṛtibhiḥ
                        kāsaharaiḥ kāsaghnaiḥ |
                        snāyucarmakhuraśṛṅgakarkaṭāsthiśuṣkamatsyavallūrakrimibhir
                        vāmanīyaiś ca vāmanīya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.5"><label>4.40.5</label> tatra bastinetravyavyair
                        dūmanetradravyāni vyākhyātāni bhavanti || dhūmanetraṃ tu
                        kanīnikāpariṇāham agre kalāyamātrasroto mūle ṅguṣṭhapariṇāhaṃ
                        dhūmavarttipraveśasroto ṅgulāni catuścatvāriṃśat prāyogike |
                        dvātriṃśat snaihike | caturviṃśati vairecanike | ṣoḍaśakāsaghne |
                        daśa vāmanīya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.6"><label>4.40.6</label> atha sukhopaviṣṭaḥ sumanā
                        ṛjvadhodṛṣṭir atandritaḥ | snehapradīptāgrām varttinetrasrotasi
                        praṇidhāya dhūmam pibed iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.7"><label>4.40.7</label> mukhena tam pibet pūrvaṃ
                        nāsikābhyān tataḥ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhapītaṃ mukhenaiva vamet pītañ ca nas tataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.8"><label>4.40.8</label> yo vamen nastato dhūman
                        nastapītaṃ mukhena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa netrakarṇṇanāsāsyasaṃśrayāl labhate gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.9"><label>4.40.9</label> viśeṣatas tu prāyogikaṃ
                        ghrāṇenādadyāt | snaihikaṃ mukhanāsābhyāṃ | nāsikābhyāṃ
                        vairecanikaṃ | mukhenaivetarāv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.11"><label>4.40.11</label> tatra
                        śramabhayāmarṣoṣṇaviṣaraktapittamadamūrcchāpipāsātāluśoṣamūrdhābhighātodgāratimiramehodarādhmānordhvavātontravṛddhibālavṛddhadurbalaviraktāsthāpitajāgaritagarbhiṇīrūkṣakṣatakṣīṇoraskāḥ
                        madhughṛtadadhidugdhamadyayavāgūpītāḥ svalpakaphāś ca dhūman na
                        severann iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.12"><label>4.40.12</label> akālapīto bhramarī
                        śirorogaṃ karoti ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāsrotokṣijihvānāṃm upaghātañ ca dāruṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.13"><label>4.40.13</label> dhūmaḥ snaihiko
                        vairecanikaḥ prāyogiko dvādaśasu kāleṣūpayogo bhavati || tad yathā
                        kṣutadantaprakṣālananasyasnānabhojanādivāsvapnamaithunacchardanamūtroccārābhir
                        uṣitaśastrakarmānteṣv iti || tasya vibhāgo
                        mūtroccārakṣavathuruṣitamaithunānteṣu snaihikaḥ |
                        divāsvapnacchardanāntayor vairecanikaḥ | dantaprakṣālanasya
                        snānabhojanaśastrakarmānteṣu prāyogika iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.14"><label>4.40.14</label> tatra snaihiko vātaṃ
                        śamayati | snehād upalepitvāc ca | vairecanikaḥ śleṣmāṇam
                        utkliśyāpakarṣati raukṣyāt taikṣṇyād auṣṇyād vaiṣadyāc ca |
                        prāyogikaḥ śleṣmāṇam utkleśayaty utkliṣṭaṃ cāpakarṣayati śamayati
                        vā sādhāraṇatvāt pūrvābhyām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.15"><label>4.40.15</label> dhūmaprayogāt puruṣaḥ
                        prasannendriyavāṅmanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛḍhakeśadvijaḥ śmaśrusugandhiviśadānanaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.16"><label>4.40.16</label> tathā
                        kāsaśvāsārocakāsyapralepasvarabhedamukhāsrāvakṣavathuvamathukrāthatandrīhanumanyāstambhapīnasaśirorogalocanaśūlāvātakaphanimittāś
                        cāsya mukharogā na bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.17"><label>4.40.17</label> tasya yogāyogātiyogā
                        vijñātavyā bhavanti | yogas tu dṛṣṭaphalārthaḥ | ayogo
                        rogānirjayaḥ | atiyogas
                        tāluśoṣaparidāhapipāsābhramamadamūrcchākarṇṇakṣveladṛṣṭirogādaurbalyayutam
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.18"><label>4.40.18</label> tatra prāyogikas trīṃs
                        trīn ucchvāsān ādadyāt paryāgatāns trīns trīṃś caturo veti ||
                        snaihikaṃ yāvad asrupravṛttiḥ || vairecanikam ādoṣadarśanāt ||
                        grāsāntareṣu kāsaharaṃ || vairecanikavat tilataṇḍulayavāgūpīto
                        vāmanīyaṃ yathāyoga iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.19"><label>4.40.19</label> tatra vraṇabastinetreṇa
                        vraṇadhūmanetraṃ vyākhyātam bhavati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śarāvasampuṭayutaṃ vraṇadhūman nayed vraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmanetreṇa matimān vedanāsrāvaśāntaye ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.20"><label>4.40.20</label> vidhir eṣa samāsena
                        dhūmasyābhihito mayā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ kuśalasammitaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.21"><label>4.40.21</label> auṣadhapakvo vā sneho
                        nāsikābhyāṃ pradīyate | nasyan tatpañcavikalpam bhavati | tad
                        yathā | nasyaṃ śirovirecanaṃ pratimarśo vapīḍaḥ pradhamanam iti |
                        teṣān nasyam pradhāṇaṃ śirovirecanaṃ yena nasya vikalpaḥ
                        pratimarśaḥ | śirovirecanavikalpo vapīḍaḥ pradhamanañ ceti | tato
                        nastaśabdaḥ pañcavidhā ṇipatati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.22"><label>4.40.22</label> tatra yaḥ snehārthaṃ
                        śūnyaśirasāṃ grīvāskandhorasāṃ balajananārthaṃ
                        dṛṣṭiprasādajananārtham vā sneha upādīyate tasmin vaiśeṣike
                        nastaśabdaḥ | tat tu deyam vātābhipanne śirasi tathā
                        dantakeśaśmasruṇātadāruṇakarṇṇakṣvelatimirasvaropaghātanāsārogamukharogaśoṣāvabāhukākālajavalīpalitaprabodheṣu
                        vātapaittikeṣu ca mukharogeṣu vātapittaharadravyasiddhena
                        sneheneti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.23"><label>4.40.23</label> śirovirecanam api
                        śleṣmaṇābhivyāptatālugataśirasāṃ tathā
                        rocakaśirogauravaśūlapīnasāvabhedakakrimipratiśyāyāpasmāraghrāṇājñāneṣv
                        anyeṣu cordhvajatrugateṣu vikāreṣu śirovirecanadravyasiddhena
                        sneheneti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.24"><label>4.40.24</label> tat tv etad dvividham
                        apy uktaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.25"><label>4.40.25</label>
                        tatroccāritavātamūtrapurīṣāya bhuktavate vyabhre kāle
                        pāṇitāpopasveditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśāya vātātaparajohīne
                        veśmany uttānaśāyine kiñcit pravilambitaśirase
                        vastrāvacchāditanetrāya vāmahastapradeśinyagronnāmitanāsāgrāya
                        viśuddhasrotase dakṣiṇahastena śuktyā picunā vā sukhoṣṇam adrutam
                        avicchinnadhārām āsiñced iti | yathā ca netreṇa prāpnoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.26"><label>4.40.26</label> snehe vasicyati śiro na
                        kathañ cana kampayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         na bhāṣen na ca kupyec ca na kṣuyān na hased api | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.27"><label>4.40.27</label> etair hi vihataḥ sneho
                        na samyak pratipadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kāsaḥ pratiśyāyaḥ śirokṣigadasambhavaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.28"><label>4.40.28</label> tasya pramāṇan tv aṣṭau
                        bindavaḥ pradeśinīparvadvayaniḥsrutāḥ | eṣā mātrā prathamā |
                        dvitīyā śuktiḥ tṛtīyā pāṇiśuktir ity etās tisro mānāḥ yathābalam
                        prayojyā bhavantīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.29"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.30"><label>4.40.30</label> śṛṅgāṭakam abhiplāvya
                        nireti vadanād yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphotkleśabhayāccainan niṣṭhīved avidhārayan || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.31"><label>4.40.31</label> dante punar api
                        saṃsvedya galakapolādīn dhūmam āseveta | bhojayec cainam
                        anabhiṣyanti | athāsyācārikam upadiśet | krodhādim pariharec ca |
                        rajodhūmamanastāpadravapānaśirasnānādīni | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.32"><label>4.40.32</label> tasya
                        yogāyogātiyogavijñānaṃ bhavati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.33"><label>4.40.33</label> lāghavaṃ śiraso yoge
                        sukhasvapnaprabodhaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vikāropaśamaḥ śuddhir indriyāṇām paraṃ sukhaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.34"><label>4.40.34</label> ayoge rogānirjayaḥ
                        kaphaprasekaḥ śiraso gurutendriyavibhramaḥ | k> atiyoge
                        tāluśoṣapipāsābhramamadamūrcchā ceti lakṣaṇam mūrdhny atisnigdhe
                        rūkṣaṃ tatrāvacārayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.35"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.36"><label>4.40.36</label> śirovirecanasyāpi
                        catvāro bindavaḥ ṣaḍ vā tathāṣṭau vā yathābalam śirovicakasnehasya
                        pramāṇam abhinirdiśet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.37"><label>4.40.37</label> tasya trīṇy
                        abhivarṇṇyante lakṣaṇāni prayogataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhihīnātisañjñāni viśeṣāc chāstracintakaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.38"><label>4.40.38</label> lāghavaṃ śirasaḥ śuddhiḥ
                        srotasāṃ vyādhinirjayaḥ | cittendriyaprasādaś ca śirasaḥ
                        śuddhilakṣaṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.39"><label>4.40.39</label> kaṇḍūpade gurutā
                        srotasāṃ kaphasambhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnāviśuddhe śirasi lakṣaṇam parikīrttitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.40"><label>4.40.40</label> mastuluṅgāgamo vā tad
                        dṛṣṭir indriyavibhramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śūnyatā śirasaś cāpi mūrdhni gāḍhavirecite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.41"><label>4.40.41</label> hīnātiśuddhe śirasi
                        kaphavātaghnam ācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag virecite cāpi sarpir naste nuṣecayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.42"><label>4.40.42</label> nasye tu parirharttavyā
                        bhavanti | tad yathā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.43"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.45"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.47"><label>4.40.47</label> bhuktavān
                        apatarpitotyarthaṃ taruṇapratiśyāyī garbhinī madyadravapīḍito
                        jīrṇṇīvastidantaḥ kruddho rāgārttaḥ tṛṣṇābhibhūto bālo vṛddhaḥ
                        śrānto vegāvarodharataḥ śirasnātukāmaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.48"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.49"><label>4.40.49</label> nasye śirovireke ca
                        vyāpado dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣotkleśakṣayāc caiva vijñeyā ca yathākramaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.50"><label>4.40.50</label> tatrotkleśanimittāsu
                        yuñjyāc chamanaśodhaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         atha kṣayanimittāsu yathāsvaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ hitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.51"><label>4.40.51</label> pratimarśes tu
                        caturdaśasu kāleṣūpadeyo bhavati | tad yathā | kālyotthitena |
                        prakṣālitadantena | gṛhān nirgacchatā | vyāyāmavyavāyapariśrātena
                        | mūtroccārakavalāṃjanānte bhuktavatā | charditavatā |
                        divāsvapnotthitena sāyañ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.52"><label>4.40.52</label> tatra
                        kālyotthitenāsevitaḥ pratimarśo rātrāv upacitaṃ nāsāsrotogataṃ
                        malam apahanti | prakṣālitadantena dantānāṃ dṛḍhatā
                        vadanasaugandhyañ cāpādayati | gṛhān nirgacchatā nāsāsrotaso
                        snehaklinnatayā | rajodhūmo vā na prabādhate |
                        vyāyāmavyavāyapariśrāntena śramam apahanti | mūtroccārānte
                        dṛṣṭigurutvam apanayati | kavalāñjanānte dṛṣṭiṃ prasādayati |
                        bhuktavatā sroto viśuddhiṃ laghutvaṃ cāpādayati | charditavatā
                        srotovilagnaṃ śleṣmāṇam apohya bhaktacchaṃdaṃ kurute |
                        divāsvapnotthitena nidrāśeṣaṃ gauravañ cāpahatya cittaikāgryaṃ
                        janayati | sāyaṃ sukhanidrāprabodham āpādayatīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.53"><label>4.40.53</label> īṣad ucchiṃghaṇāt sneho
                        yadā vaktum prapadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         naste niśiktaṃ taṃ vidyāt pratimarśaṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.54"><label>4.40.54</label> tena rogāḥ praśāmyanti
                        narāṇām ūrdhvajatrujāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         indriyāṇāñ ca vaimalyaṃ kuryād āsyasugandhi ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.55"><label>4.40.55</label>
                        hanudantaśirogrīvātrikabāhūrasāṃ balaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         valīpalitakhālityavyaṃgānāñ cāpy asambhavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.56"><label>4.40.56</label> tailaṃ kaphe ca vāte ca
                        kevalaṃ pavane vasāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyān nastaḥ sadā pitte sarpirmajjāsamārute || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.57"><label>4.40.57</label> caturvidhasya snehasya
                        vidhir eṣa prakīrttitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmasthānāvirodhitvāt teṣu tailaṃ viśiṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44"><label>4.40.44</label> avapīḍan tu
                        śirovirecanavad abhiṣyaṇṇasarpadaṣṭamūrcchitavisaṃjñebhyo dadyāc
                        chirovirecanadravyāṇām anyatamam āsādyāvapīḍam iṣyateti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.46"><label>4.40.46</label> cetovikārakrimiviṣād iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44a"><label>4.40.44a</label> śarkarekṣurasakṣīrā
                        ghṛtamāṃsarasāṃ pṛthak kṣīṇānāṃ nastato dadyādd raktapittagadeṣu
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.58"><label>4.40.58</label> ataḥ param pravakṣyāmi
                        kavaḍagrahaṇe vidhiṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturdhā kavaḍasnehī prasādī śodhiropaṇau | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.59"><label>4.40.59</label> sngidhoṣṇaiḥ snaihiko
                        vāte svāduśītaiḥ prasādanaḥ pitte kaṭvamblalavaṇai rūkṣaiḥ
                        saṃśodhaṇaḥ kaphe | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.60"><label>4.40.60</label> kaṣāyatiktamadhuraiḥ
                        kaṭūṣṇo ropaṇo vraṇe | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.61"><label>4.40.61</label> tatra
                        trikaṭukāśitasarṣapasiddhārthakakalkam āloḍya
                        tailamūtrakṣārasurāśuktamadhūnām anyatamena salavaṇam
                        abhiprataptam upasvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśe dhārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.62"><label>4.40.62</label> sukhaṃ sañcāryate yā tu
                        mātrā sā kavalaḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         asañcāryā tu yā mātrā gaṇḍūṣaḥ sā prakīrttitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.63"><label>4.40.63</label> tāvac ca dhārayitavyo
                        nanyamanasānunnatadehena yāvad doṣapratipūrṇṇagalakapolatvaṃ
                        nāsāsrotonayanapariplavaś ca bhavati tadā vimoktavyaḥ | punaś
                        cānyo grahītavyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.64"><label>4.40.64</label> evaṃ
                        snehapayaḥkṣaudrarasamūtrāmblasambhṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kasāyoṣṇodakābhyāñ ca kavaḍā doṣato hitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.65"><label>4.40.65</label> vyādher apacayas tuṣṭir
                        viṣadaṃ vaktralāghavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         indriyāṇām prasādaś ca kavaḍe śuddhilakṣaṇaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.66"><label>4.40.66</label> hīne jāḍyakaphotkleśā
                        varasajñānam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         atiyogāt mukhe pākaḥ śoṣas tṛṣṇāruciklamaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.67"><label>4.40.67</label> śodhanīye viśeṣeṇa
                        bhavaty etat tu lakṣaṇaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tilāṃ nīlotpalaṃ sarpiḥ śarkarā kṣīram eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.68"><label>4.40.68</label> sakṣaudro
                        dagdhavarktrasya gaṇḍūṣo dāhanāśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kavalasya samāsena vidhir eṣaḥ prakīrttitaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.69"><label>4.40.69</label> vibhajya bheṣajaṃ budhyā
                        kurvīta pratisāraṇaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kalko rasakriyā kṣaudraṃ cūrṇṇañ ceti caturvidhaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.70"><label>4.40.70</label> aṅgulyagrapraṇītan tu
                        yathāsvam mukharogiṇāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya yogam ayogañ ca kavaloktaṃ vibhāvayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.71"><label>4.40.71</label> bhojayet cānabhiṣyandi
                        doṣaghnam aśanaṃ naram iti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer"> || ci 40 || 0 || </p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.72"><label>4.40.72</label> sneha svedo vamanaṃ
                        virekaṃ vyāpadaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         netre pramāṇa vyāpac cānuvāsanasahottaraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.73"><label>4.40.73</label> nirūhottarapīḍā ca
                        dhūmanastena vai daśa || ❈ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.74"><label>4.40.74</label>yad uktañ catvāriṃśac
                        cikitsitānīti tat sarvaṃ samāptam iti || ❈ ||</l>
